memos always come from `desc`. **`--anonymize`** hashes payees + memos (sha256 first-8-bytes hex) so a shareable sample db carries no real names/notes. **`make fixture`** wired: builds `bin/ledgerimport`, `rm`s any stale `fixtures/sample.db`, runs `build` against the gitignored `fixtures/source/{jrnl.csv,mapping-accounts.csv,mapping.json}` with `--anonymize` (paths overridable) -- LOCAL-ONLY, never in `make test`/CI, the p09.4 human-run step. **ALL tests use SYNTHETIC data (rule 11):** parser tests feed invented 22-field lines (quoted multi-line memos, dot-decimal amounts, garbage-filled float-noisy net columns asserted IGNORED, a multi-currency tid); `TestMappingAppliesSubFundProgramFunction` builds a tiny synthetic org and asserts sub/fund/program/functional defaults applied; `TestImportedBooksBalance` builds into a temp db and asserts `ledger.Check` has ZERO Error violations, the multi-currency tid produced TWO FX-clearing-paired txns, Opening Balances absorbed the opening group, and the consolidation-marker row was skipped; a `--anonymize` test asserts no produced payee/memo equals a synthetic original. Tests-first (observed): with `runAccounts`/`runBuild`/`BuildResult` undefined the package failed to compile ("undefined: runBuild" etc.) -- the right reason -- then implementing turned all 8 green. No new dependency; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged (`make gen` reproducible); `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists).
- **p26.12** — Account tree DERIVED from `stmt` + `typ` as a two-level chain, superseding the explicit `parent` column. The `accounts` skeleton (`runAccounts`, `cmd/ledgerimport/accounts.go`) now builds `<stmt super-parent> -> <(stmt,typ) intermediate> -> <leaf>` (e.g. Assets → Bank → BOA Checking) instead of setting each leaf's `cuento_parent` from the `parent` COLUMN. It synthesizes the intermediate + super-parent rows into the reviewable account-mapping CSV, so `build.go` (which sees only the reviewed CSV, no `typ`, and already topo-sorts arbitrary parent chains parent-before-child) needs ZERO change. **stmt → super-parent NAME** (`stmtToSuperParent` in mapping.go, mirroring `stmtToType`): `A/L/I/E/O → Assets/Liabilities/Revenue/Expenses/Equity` — the balance-sheet/activity report section names, so the imported chart's top tier reads like the reports (the pre-existing accounts_test already expected "Assets"/"Expenses"). **Intermediates keyed by `(cuento-type, typ)`, not `typ` alone** (`typParentKey`) — the same `typ` under two `stmt` supertypes (the existing synthetic data has one) yields two DISTINCT tiers (Assets→Bank ≠ Expenses→Bank), which for free enforces **type consistency**: a leaf always nests under an intermediate of its own stmt type (prefer the leaf's own stmt). **Synthetic parents are namespaced** — their account-map KEY (`source_acct`, which `build.go` resolves `cuento_parent` against) carries a reserved `::super:` / `::typ:` prefix (`superParentKey`/`typParentKey`) that a real org `acct` path can never match, so a leaf literally named the same as a `typ` value or a super-parent name never collides; the human-facing `name_en`/`name_es` stay the clean names. **Subsidiary unions are TWO-PASS (the load-bearing correctness point):** `typ` is documented as a PER-JOURNAL-ENTRY classification, so one `acct` recurs under many typs and its country union accrues from all of them, while its parent chain is fixed at FIRST sighting (file order — deterministic tie-break). A per-record accumulation would leave a country on the leaf but not on its chosen parent, violating rule 7 / Z12 (and `build.go`/`CreateAccount` + `cuento check` reject a parent whose subs are not a superset of its children's — `main.go`'s build runs `ledger.Check` and exits nonzero). So pass 2 propagates each leaf's FULL subsidiary union UP its chosen chain (bounded walk of `CuentoParent` keys). Regression `TestRunAccountsLeafSpansTypsSubsetSubs` (same acct as (A,Bank,US) then (A,Transfer,MX)) asserts the chosen intermediate + super-parent are supersets of the leaf's {US,MX}. **Edge cases (comment + docs):** blank `typ` → leaf directly under the super-parent (tier skipped); a `typ` whose normalized text equals the super-parent's own name → tier collapsed (no self-parent); blank/unknown `stmt` → leaf left top-level for review; a leaf literally NAMED like a super-parent or a typ value coexists as an ordinary leaf (namespaced keys, no collision). **Surfaced for human review (task "deterministic and reviewable"):** because `typ` is per-journal-entry, which typ names a leaf's parent is semantically arbitrary — flagged in `docs/ledger-export.md` alongside the first-sighting tie-break, for the go-live review to confirm the tier names read sensibly. **Explicit `parent` column: IGNORED for structure** (simplest correct behavior — the stmt/typ chain is authoritative and the go-live mapping gets human review regardless; stated in `docs/ledger-export.md`). This supersedes the p09.4 "account tree = 59 source `parent` grouping paths materialized as placeholders" note — the placeholder tier is now the stmt/typ two-level chain. Tests-first (observed): `TestRunAccountsEmitsTwoLevelChain` + `TestRunAccountsTypCollidesWithLeafName` failed on undefined `typParentKey`/`superParentKey`, then green; `build_test.go` (hand-built explicit `AccountMap` chains) needed NO change. `go vet ./...`, `gofmt -l cmd/ledgerimport`, `go test ./cmd/ledgerimport/...`, `make test` all clean; no new dependency.
- **p09.4** — Go-live import rehearsal with a **best-guess autonomous mapping** (human authorized); the reviewed mapping, `cuento check --strict`, and the spreadsheet spot-check remain human gates before cutover (see `docs/golive.md`). **Result: `cuento check -db fixtures/sample.db` = 0 Errors, 151 Warnings (all Z19 unmapped-990)** — the non-strict go-live goal. Build aggregates: 3 subsidiaries / 1 program (root "General") / 0 funds / 293 accounts (232 leaves + 59 parent placeholders + 2 synthetic import accounts); ~42.1k non-consolidation source `tid` groups → ~49.5k cuento transactions (~34.6k single-currency direct + ~7.6k multi-currency decomposed through FX Clearing into paired single-currency txns, D3); ~1.0k non-balancing single-currency groups routed their residual to per-subsidiary Opening Balances as counted warnings (hazard #4, never force-balanced); consolidation-marker rows skipped. **Two committed code changes, both generic + synthetic-test-covered (rule 11):** (1) **HNL currency seed** — the source's local currency (Honduran Lempira, ISO 4217 exponent 2) was absent from the p03.1 seed; a new forward migration `00011_currency_hnl.sql` seeds it (rule 4: never edit 00003; forward-only, no down), without which the HNL subsidiary's `base_currency` FK and every HNL split fail. `TestSeedCurrencies` extended to assert HNL present. (2) **Source dimensions gated by account type** — `resolveSplit` forwarded the source `kls` (functional class) to EVERY split and `kat` (program) whenever mapped, but the export populates `kls` on non-expense lines (~72k) and `kat` on non-R/E lines (~52k); the store rejects a functional class off an expense account (`ErrNonExpenseFunction`) and a program on a balance-sheet split (`ErrProgramOnBalanceSheet`), which was dropping ~43k transactions. Fix: the builder records each created account's cuento type (`builder.acctType`), and `resolveSplit` applies `kls`→functional class ONLY on expense splits and `kat`→program ONLY on R/E splits; the store's own account-default path fills the rest. Covered by `TestSourceDimensionsGatedByAccountType` (a synthetic revenue+asset pair that both carry `kls` and `kat` and must post with NULL functional_class / NULL program). **Best-guess mapping decisions (flagged for human review in docs/golive.md, values kept in the gitignored `fixtures/source/mapping-notes.md`):** subsidiary names (placeholders); functional-class 4→3 enum mapping (D21); **program handling = simplest** (all R/E on root "General", no `kat`→program mapping — richer option left for the human, D24); **funds = none** (all unrestricted, donors not yet named, D20); **990 codes = none** (→ the 151 Z19 warnings, D25); **account tree** = 59 source parent grouping paths materialized as type-pure placeholder accounts with subsidiary set = union of children (superset invariant Z12), one CONS-only leaf mapped to root as a fallback (no splits); consolidation rows skipped; imbalance→Opening Balances; no payees. **Real data never entered the repo (rule 11):** `fixtures/source/{jrnl.csv,mapping.json,mapping-accounts.csv,mapping-notes.md}` and `fixtures/sample.db` are all gitignored (verified `git check-ignore`); only structural descriptions and aggregate counts appear in committed docs. `make check` passes on the CI path (no `fixtures/sample.db` present); locally with the sample db present it additionally runs `--strict`, which by design fails on the 151 Z19 warnings (the human-review gate). `make lint test`, `go vet`, `govulncheck ./...` exit 0; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged (no new dependency).
- **p10.2** — Base layout + theme + i18n wiring + CSS foundation. **`base.tmpl` is the shared shell**, split into reusable partials (`shell-open`/`shell-close` frame the `<html>…<main>` document; `shell-nav`, `theme-control`). html/template shares ONE parse set, so a page cannot override a shared "content" block (a redefinition error at parse); instead each shell page (`base.tmpl` landing, `settings.tmpl`, `styleguide.tmpl`, `admin.tmpl`) is a self-contained top-level template that emits `shell-open`, its own `<main>` body, then `shell-close`. A tiny `shellTitle` template func pairs the `shellPage` model (`.Shell` chrome + `.Page`) with a per-page localized head title so the frame stays shared while each page's `<title>` is a real `{{t}}` string. **Theme is SSR / flash-free:** `resolveTheme` reads the `cuento_theme` cookie first (set the instant the user toggles), else the logged-in user's persisted `theme` setting, else `"auto"` — all server-side, so `<html data-theme=…>` is correct in the first byte with no client round-trip and no flash. An unrecognized cookie value is ignored (falls through), so a tampered cookie can't inject arbitrary attribute text. `CurrentUser` gained a `Theme` field (via `UserByID`) for the logged-in-no-cookie fallback. **`POST /theme` (AnyUser):** validates the value against `store.ValidTheme` (light/dark/auto), sets the cookie (HttpOnly — no JS reads it, SSR only; `Secure` off only in `-dev`; SameSite=Lax; 1-year), and for a logged-in user persists `SetUserTheme` through the write funnel (one audited change, `theme` IS in the users_versions snapshot). PRG: 303 back to a **same-origin** Referer (`sameOriginPath` blocks open-redirects — leading single "/", no scheme/host, not "//"), else "/". **Data-driven perm-gated nav:** `navSections()` is an ordered table of `{LabelKey, Href, Perm}` for the Appendix-F top-level sections; `visibleNav` renders an entry only when its route is **registered** (`registeredGetPaths()` derived from `routes()` — no dead links) AND the user **satisfies** its Perm (reusing the p06.3 `decide` policy so nav visibility and route enforcement can never disagree; the `ReportGroup` reports entry means "any grant or admin" for nav, the concrete report routes gate per group in p15). p11–p18 append their nav entry when they register their route — the entry lights up automatically, no nav edit. **Recorded scope choice — a minimal `GET /admin` stub (Admin):** the DoD requires proving "Admin sees the admin entry, a non-admin does not", but the no-dead-links rule hides the admin section until `/admin` exists. Registering a minimal Admin-only landing stub (parallel to the required `/settings` stub — both render through the shell, are localized, and give the nav a real permitted target) is the smallest reversible way to make the admin gate real and testable now; the real admin pages (users, subsidiaries, currencies, ops) still land in p11.3/p13.2/p14.2/p18.3. So this step registers **four** routes, not three: `POST /theme`, `GET /settings`, `GET /admin` (all in the matrix), plus `GET /styleguide` **only in `-dev`** (absent from the registry — and thus 404 — in production; Public so a designer views it login-free). **Login language switcher:** plain `<a ?lang=…>` links (no JS, CSP-safe); the lang middleware already honors `?lang` (D14), each language labelled in its OWN tongue (`lang.<code>` identical across catalogs). **CSS foundation (`static/app.css`, hand-written, strict-CSP: styles live only in the file, never inline):** three layers — TOKENS (CSS custom properties), RESET, COMPONENT primitives. Light/dark via `color-scheme` + `light-dark()`: every theme token is a `light-dark(light, dark)` pair and `color-scheme` (set per `data-theme` on `<html>`: `auto`→`light dark`, `light`/`dark`→the fixed side) selects the active side — no media query, no JS. **No hand-written JS this step** (the theme toggle is a plain `<form>` POST), so no `node --test` unit was needed and the boring-frontend/CSP surface stays minimal. **e2e:** `e2e/tests/shell.spec.js` logs in via the harness fixture, asserts the shell landmarks + a localized nav label, toggles the theme and asserts `data-theme` changes and **persists across a reload** (SSR from the cookie), and checks the login page localizes to Spanish via the switcher; `make e2e` green (6 specs: 3 login + 3 shell). **Tests-first (observed):** the new `shell_test.go` failed to compile — `undefined: themeCookieName` and the not-yet-registered `/theme`/`/settings`/`/styleguide` routes / missing `base.tmpl` — the right reason; implementing turned every listed test green (`TestThemeCookieSSR`, `TestNavLocalized`, `TestNavPermGated`, `TestHTMLLangMatchesLocale`, `TestSettingsStubRendersShell`, `TestThemePersistsCookieAndSetting`, `TestStyleguideDevOnly`), and the pre-existing `TestCatalogParity`, permission-matrix, and asset/login tests still pass (the new routes flow through the matrix automatically). No new dependency; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged; `make gen` reproducible (one query `SetUserTheme` + `UserByID` gains `theme`); `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make e2e` green.
- **p10.3** — htmx wiring + the reusable form-error convention every later form (accounts p11, transactions p12, reconciliation p16, import p17) inherits. **Vendored pinned htmx 2.0.4** (`internal/web/static/htmx.min.js`, SHA-256 `e209dda5c8235479f3166defc7750e1dbcd5a5c1808b7792fc2e6733768fb447`, 50917 bytes) — fetched ONCE to vendor, verified byte-identical across two independent CDNs (jsdelivr, unpkg) before committing; served locally through the p10.1 asset pipeline under the strict `script-src 'self'` CSP (rule 12, NO CDN at runtime, tests never hit the network). The version+hash live in `internal/web/VENDOR.md`, kept OUTSIDE `static/` deliberately so `buildAssetManifest` (which hashes every file under `static/`) does not serve/hash the note. Loaded in `base.tmpl`'s `<head>` via `<script src="{{asset "htmx.min.js"}}" defer>` (hashed/immutable in prod, unhashed in `-dev`); **not a Go dependency** (a static asset), `go.mod`/`go.sum` untouched. **Two htmx-config settings, set CSP-safely via a `<meta name="htmx-config">` (never inline script) BEFORE htmx loads:** (1) **`responseHandling` adds `{"code":"422","swap":true}` before the `[45]..` error rule** — htmx 2.x does NOT swap 4xx/5xx by default (it fires `htmx:responseError`), but the form-error convention returns **422** and MUST swap the form-region partial, so 422 is whitelisted for swap (first match wins; 2xx/3xx keep default swap, 204 no-swap, other 4xx/5xx stay error). Without this the Go 422 test passes but the e2e swap silently fails — so the **e2e is the load-bearing proof**, not the Go test. (2) **`includeIndicatorStyles:false`** — htmx otherwise injects an inline `<style>` on load, which `style-src 'self'` (no unsafe-inline) would block with a console CSP error on every page; any indicator CSS goes in `app.css`. **`hx-boost` scope = the top-level nav ONLY** (`<nav class="app-nav" hx-boost="true">` in `shell-nav`): progressive enhancement — the `<a href>` nav links still do full-page navigation without JS; with htmx they become targeted body swaps. Boost is NOT on `<header>`, the logout form, the theme form, or page content (task: nav only). **Form-error convention (the reusable pattern):** a form's markup is a **SINGLE-SOURCED named partial** (demonstrator: `"demo-form"` in `templates/formdemo.tmpl`, `hx-post`+`hx-target="#demo-form"`+`hx-swap="outerHTML"`). The full page renders it inside the shell (`{{template "demo-form" .Page}}`); a failed POST re-renders **JUST that partial** — so input ids (`demo-name`/`demo-email`) stay **stable across the swap** (anti-jank, Appendix C) with zero duplicated markup. On invalid input the handler returns **HTTP 422** via the thin reusable helper **`renderFormError(w, r, partial, model)`** (a 422 + partial-name + model over the existing `render`, which already sets no-store and rebinds `{{t}}`/`{{asset}}` for the request language). **Field errors are i18n KEYS** (rule 9: Go returns keys) held in an **ordered `formErrors`** value (`.add(field, key)` in field order); the template renders each via `{{t .}}` and stamps **`autofocus` on `FirstInvalid()` ONLY** — the first (top-most) invalid field — so focus lands on the first problem. Reusable field validators return keys: `requiredKey`/`emailKey` → `error.required`/`error.email` (both catalogs). **Demonstrator = a POST on the `-dev`-only `/styleguide`** (Public): a genuine handler (`styleguideSubmit`) going through the real registry + middleware, validating Name (required) + Email (required + plausible), returning **422 + the partial** on invalid input and **200 + the partial with a success message** on valid input. Chosen `-dev`-only so no demo endpoint exists in production and it never enters the permission matrix (parallels the p10.2 `-dev` styleguide GET); a permanent AnyUser POST was equally sanctioned. **`formfocus.js`** (small hand-written ES module, external so it loads under `script-src 'self'` — NO inline handler): browsers don't fire `autofocus` on nodes inserted by a swap, so on `htmx:afterSwap` it focuses the first `[autofocus]` in the swapped region; the pure helper (`firstAutofocus`/`focusFirstAutofocus`) is **unit-tested with `node --test`** (`formfocus.test.js`, 6 cases, stub nodes, no jsdom/no dep), the browser glue a thin guarded shim. **Makefile `test`** now passes `node --test` the `*.test.js` **globs** (not the bare directory — recent Node treats a directory arg as a module to run), so the JS unit suite is discovered. **Tests-first (observed):** `TestFormErrorPartial` first failed with `POST /styleguide status = 405` (the demonstrator route/handler didn't exist yet — GET-only) — the right reason; implementing turned it green (422 = fragment not full page, localized en+es errors resolved via catalog not raw keys, exactly one `autofocus` on the first invalid field, valid POST → 200 not 422). `TestCatalogParity` stays green with the new keys in both catalogs. **e2e** `e2e/tests/formerror.spec.js` (2 specs) drives the real `/styleguide`: an invalid submit swaps the 422 partial IN PLACE (a `window` sentinel survives → **no full reload**), the localized field error is visible, focus lands on the first invalid field; a valid submit swaps in the success message. `make e2e` green (8 specs: 3 login + 3 shell + 2 form-error).  **`*.test.js` excluded from the served assets:** the JS unit test rides along in `//go:embed static` (embed can't filter by suffix), so `buildAssetManifest` and `staticHandler` both skip `*.test.js` (via `isTestAsset`) — test code is never hashed, manifested, or reachable on the Public `/static` URL (rule 12; `TestJSUnitTestNotServed` locks it in, `TestVendoredHtmxServed` proves the real htmx asset serves). `make gen` reproducible (no query change); `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
- **p11.1** — Chart of accounts (`/accounts`), the first big feature page + the template every later CRUD page follows. **Store is the sole validator (rule 8/2):** the handler never re-checks tree/990/sub rules — it parses the form, calls `CreateAccount`/`UpdateAccount`/`SetAccountName`/`SetAccountSubsidiaries`/`DeactivateAccount`, and on a TYPED store error `accountErrorField` maps it to a `(form field, i18n key)` pair, then `renderFormError` re-renders the `account-form` partial at **422** with `autofocus` on that field (the p10.3 convention, REUSED not re-implemented). Every typed error is mapped to an `error.account.*` key in both catalogs (`ErrNameRequired`→name_en, `ErrNoSubsidiary`→subs, `ErrCrossTypeClass`/`ErrCycle`/`ErrSubMismatch`/`ErrAccountNotFound`→parent_id, `Err990TypeMismatch`→form990_code, `ErrFunctionalClassNotExpense`→functional_class, `ErrDefaultProgramNotRE/Missing/Inactive`→default_program, `ErrSubInUseByChild`→subs). **Filtered options live in the STORE, reusing the write-path predicates** (so offered options and accepted writes can never disagree): `ParentOptions(lang,type,excludeID)` returns tree-ordered accounts EXCLUDING self+descendants (via `AccountDescendants`) AND type-incompatible parents (via the same `typeCompatible` the move validates with); `Form990LinesForType(type)` filters the seeded lines by CSV membership reusing `csvContains` (extracted from `check990Type` so ONE predicate serves both) + a new `ListForm990Lines` sqlc query; the subsidiary filter is just `Tree(lang,&sub)`. `TestParentOptionsExcludeDescendantsAndWrongClass`/`TestForm990OptionsFilteredByType`/`TestSubsidiaryFilter` assert on these DATA STRUCTURES, not scraped HTML. **Balances match p08.4 exactly:** `balancesByAccount(ctx,st,asof,scopeSub)` is exposed as a plain function (asof/scope explicit) so `TestBalancesColumnMatchesQuery` asserts equality against `SubtreeBalancesAsOf(sameDate,scope)` with no `time.Now`/HTML dependence; the numbers come STRAIGHT from the query, the function only attaches each currency's exponent for the money formatter. Default (no sub filter) balance scope = the **root subsidiary** (full consolidation, D18), derived from `SubTree()`'s NULL-parent row. **Rule 10 plumbing (the recorded extension):** the money formatters need the user's number/neg/display/date settings, but `CurrentUser` (and `UserByID`) carried only locale/theme — so this step extends the un-pinned `UserByID` projection + `CurrentUser` with `date_format/number_format/display_mode/neg_style` (DB defaults US/signed/minus/ISO apply to any untouched session, so no existing test breaks; the pinned `GetUser` is untouched) and adds `internal/web/format.go` (`formatOptsFor`/`dateFormatFor`, string→`money.FormatOpts`/`DateFormat`) — the single settings→formatter mapping p13.1 reuses. **Move-to-top-level is not offered (recorded limitation):** `UpdateAccount` treats a non-nil `ParentID` as a MOVE target and has no way to express "move to NULL/top-level" (a non-nil 0 resolves to non-existent account id 0 → `ErrAccountNotFound`); so the handler sends `ParentID` only when the selection is **positive** — a positive parent moves, selecting "top level" is a no-op reparent (an account already at top level stays there; re-homing a child up to top level is a store gap left for a later step, not invented here). **Edit is multiple store calls, not atomic across them:** `UpdateAccount` (move/flags/990/program, the most-likely-to-fail) runs FIRST so its typed error maps cleanly, then `SetAccountName`×2, then `SetAccountSubsidiaries` (which propagates the assigned subs UP the ancestor chain, D18 — surfaced in the form via a hint string and proven by `TestSubAssignmentPropagation`); create IS atomic (one `CreateAccount` change). **htmx success = HX-Redirect (the load-bearing UX fix):** the inline form posts with `hx-target="#account-form" hx-swap="outerHTML"`, so a plain 303 would swap the whole `/accounts` page INTO the small form region; `redirectAfterForm` instead sets **`HX-Redirect`** (204) on an htmx request so htmx does a full-page navigation reloading the tree, and falls back to a 303 PRG when JS is off. **Type-change value preservation:** the type `<select>` re-fetches the form (`hx-get` + `hx-include="closest form"`) so the type-dependent regions (functional class shown only on expense, default program only on R/E, filtered 990/parent options) refresh; `overlayFormValues` overlays the in-flight query params onto the rebuilt form so switching type never wipes what the user typed. **Only send type-gated fields:** functional class is sent only when type=expense, default program only when type∈{revenue,expense} — else the store's early `ErrFunctionalClassNotExpense`/`ErrDefaultProgramNotRE` would fire on the happy path. **CSP-clean (rule 12):** tree indentation is `acct-depth-N` CSS classes (NOT an inline `style` attribute, which `style-src 'self'` blocks); Cancel is a plain `<a href>` (NOT an `hx-on:click` inline handler); a `strs` template func supplies the static type/functional-class enums so the value lists stay out of the page model. **Routes registered (rule 8, matrix picks them up):** `GET /accounts` (TxnRead), `GET /accounts/new`, `GET /accounts/{id}/edit`, `POST /accounts`, `POST /accounts/{id}`, `POST /accounts/{id}/deactivate` (all TxnWrite). The `nav.accounts` entry (already seeded in `shell.go`) lights up now that GET `/accounts` exists — no nav edit needed. `newMatrixApp` (test harness) now seeds one account so the `{id}`-parameterized routes resolve to a real resource under the reachability check (the harness's stated forward-compatibility intent for p12's register/history). **Edit-error re-render threads the id (a caught defect):** `parseAccountForm(r, id)` takes the edit id (0 = create) and passes it to `buildAccountForm`, so a 422 re-render of an EDIT rebuilds the parent select with self+descendants excluded and shows the inherited 990 code — a first cut hardcoded id=0 there, which would have offered the account itself as its own parent on an error re-render (invisible to the happy-path tests); `TestAccountsEditErrorReRenderExcludesSelf` locks it in (verified failing when reverted to id=0). **Tests-first (observed):** the two new store methods neutered to `return nil, nil` made `TestParentOptionsExcludeDescendantsAndWrongClass` (new-revenue options empty) and `TestForm990OptionsFilteredByType` (every type "returned no lines") fail on assertions — the right reason (`TestSubsidiaryFilter` is green throughout since it reuses the existing `Tree`, an inherent not-red case, noted here per AGENTS rule 1); the web handler tests failed to compile (`undefined: balancesByAccount`) then 404'd until the routes registered, then went green. **e2e** `e2e/tests/accounts.spec.js` (3 specs): admin logs in, creates an account through the REAL inline htmx form and asserts it in the tree, edits it, and a blank-name submit shows the localized inline field error (form-error convention). `make e2e` green (11 specs). `TestCatalogParity` stays green with the new `accounts.*`/`account.type.*`/`functional.*`/`error.account.*` keys. `make gen` reproducible (two queries added: `ListForm990Lines`, `UserByID` projection); `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
- **p11.2** — Merge UI (`/accounts/merge`, TxnWrite), plugged into the p11.1 accounts page as a second `#account-form` trigger ("Merge accounts") beside "New account". **Two-step, confirm-required flow:** `GET /accounts/merge` renders the `merge-form` partial (source + destination pickers listing only ACTIVE LEAF accounts, since `MergeAccount` requires both to be leaves, D11); `POST /accounts/merge` WITHOUT a `confirm` flag renders the `merge-preview` partial — a consequences summary (how many transaction lines repoint, `0` reconciliations move, the source is deactivated) plus a Confirm control — and performs **zero writes**; a second POST WITH `confirm=1` executes `store.MergeAccount`. `TestMergeConfirmRequired` proves the no-confirm branch does not repoint/deactivate. **Validate at CONFIRM, never a dry-run (the recorded design choice):** there is no rollback-only path and duplicating the store's checks would violate rule 8/the p11.1 "store is the sole validator" convention, so the merge's legality (cross-type, sub-coverage, leaf/placeholder/inactive/self) surfaces on the confirm POST — `MergeAccount` validates-then-writes atomically, so a typed error means nothing was written and "no execution" holds trivially; the handler maps each sentinel to an i18n key and re-renders `merge-form` at **422** (the p10.3 convention, REUSED). The preview still RESTATES the coverage rule as an informational note (`merge.coverage_note`), separate from the error message. **All SIX sentinels mapped** (`mergeErrorField`, mirroring `accountErrorField`) so no legitimate rejection falls through to the 500 path: `ErrMergeSelf`/`ErrMergeNotLeaf`/`ErrMergeCrossTypeClass`/`ErrMergeSubsetSubs`→src select, `ErrMergeIntoPlaceholder`/`ErrMergeIntoInactive`→dst select; a missing selection is a client-side `error.merge.select_both` on src. **Preview count == merge effect BY CONSTRUCTION:** new read helper `store.SplitIDsForAccount` calls the SAME `SplitIdsByAccount` query `MergeAccount` repoints from (NOT deleted-filtered — it moves soft-deleted-txn splits too, per that query's comment), so the previewed split count can never drift from what actually moves; `len()` is the count. **Routes (rule 8, matrix auto-covers):** `GET`+`POST /accounts/merge` (both TxnWrite); the literal `/accounts/merge` is more specific than `/accounts/{id}`, so the Go 1.22+ mux routes it precisely with no conflict/panic (mount + matrix tests confirm). `TestMergePermissions` keeps the explicit ReadOnly-403 / anon-302 assertions the step lists (partly redundant with the matrix). **Tests-first (observed):** the handler tests first failed to COMPILE (`st.SplitIDsForAccount undefined`) — the right reason (the read helper, route, handler and partials all did not exist yet); implementing the two-step handler + partials + route turned all six green (happy path repoints+deactivates via the store; confirm-required does nothing; consequences show the split count + 0-recon note; sub-coverage and cross-type return 422 with the localized message and no execution). **e2e** `e2e/tests/merge.spec.js` creates two expense leaves through the real UI, reviews the consequences, confirms, and asserts the source drops out of the active-only tree while the destination survives. `make e2e` green (12 specs). `TestCatalogParity` stays green with the new `accounts.merge`/`merge.*`/`error.merge.*` keys in both catalogs. `make gen` reproducible (**no query change** — the read helper reuses the existing `SplitIdsByAccount`); `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.

- **p11.3** — `/admin/subsidiaries` (Perm **Admin**, Appendix B/F) is the p11.1 accounts page recut for a currency-carrying single-root tree: `subsidiaries.go` renders the depth-indented `store.SubTree` list (name / base currency / active) with an inline htmx create/edit form (name, parent, base currency) and a deactivate action; `subsidiaries.tmpl` + `subsidiary_form.tmpl` mirror `accounts.tmpl`/`account_form.tmpl`. **No new store/SQL** — every method (`SubTree`, `GetSubsidiary`, `Descendants`, `CreateSubsidiary`, `UpdateSubsidiary`, `DeactivateSubsidiary`, `Currencies`) already existed, so `make gen` is a no-op and `go.mod` is unchanged. The handler **never re-validates** (rule: store owns validation); it maps the store's typed errors to i18n keys: create-with-no-parent → `ErrSecondRoot`→`error.subsidiary.second_root`, giving the root a parent → `ErrRootImmovable`→`error.subsidiary.root_immovable`, a descendant move → `ErrCycle`→`error.subsidiary.cycle` (**`ErrCycle` is the SHARED sentinel** accounts moves also return — same physical error, subsidiary-specific key), missing parent → `ErrParentMissing`→`error.subsidiary.parent_missing`; all re-render the form partial at 422. **Deactivate deviates from accounts' deactivate** (which 500s on unknown / 404s on missing): a blocked deactivate (`ErrHasActiveChildren`) re-renders the LIST at 422 with a page-level `error.subsidiary.has_active_children` alert, and the store's no-trace discipline leaves the subsidiary active (the test asserts both). The parent select excludes the subject + `Descendants(id)` and is omitted for the root (presentation only; the store still enforces). The `/admin` landing (`admin.tmpl`) links the page; the six routes go in `routes.go` under Admin so the permission matrix picks them up (matrix hits `/admin/subsidiaries/1/...` on the childless root, so every path is non-404/non-403 for Admin). New `subsidiaries.*`/`error.subsidiary.*` keys added to BOTH catalogs (`TestCatalogParity` green). **Login rate-limiter bypassed in `-dev`** (`login.go`): the limiter (burst 5 per ip+user) exists to choke online password guessing in production; `-dev` is a local, non-adversarial mode (it already relaxes the session-cookie Secure flag for the same reason), and the worker-scoped Playwright suite drives many rapid same-user logins against one `-dev` server that the burst would otherwise throttle into intermittent login-bounce failures (a pre-existing fragility this step exposed). Guarded strictly on `cfg.Dev`; `TestLoginRateLimited` runs `Dev=false` and stays green, so the production guarantee is untouched. `make e2e` green (`e2e/tests/subsidiaries.spec.js`: one login, then create-child → rename → blocked-deactivate). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
- **p11.4** — Org settings & languages. **`org_settings(key TEXT PRIMARY KEY, value TEXT NOT NULL)`** (migration `00012`) is a simple NON-versioned CONFIG table — absent from Appendix A's versions list, exactly like `currencies`/`report_groups`: no `org_settings_versions`, no trigger, no `changes` wiring. Seeded `org_name` (empty) and `enabled_languages` (`en,es`). Store helpers `OrgSetting(key,def)`/`SetOrgSetting(key,value)`/`EnabledLanguages()` are plain sqlc reads + an idempotent upsert **outside the write funnel** (rule 2 permits config upserts via sqlc without an actor/changes row) — the `/admin/org` handler therefore does NOT use `actorCtx`: these are configuration writes, not audited business mutations. **Report base currency is intentionally NOT an org setting** — it follows the scoped subsidiary's `base_currency` (D18), so it lives on `subsidiaries`, not here. **`en` is always an enabled name language (smallest-choice, recorded):** `EnabledLanguages` guarantees `en` present and FIRST even if an admin drops it from the stored CSV (parse: split on comma, trim, drop blanks, dedupe, prepend `en`) — the required base name (p05.3 fallback) must always have an input; a now-disabled language's stored `account_names` rows are left alone (fallback still uses them). The enabled-languages value is stored VERBATIM and normalized only at read time, so a stray space or dropped `en` never breaks the account form. **Account name inputs are enabled-languages-driven (the p11.4 payoff):** `accountForm.NameEN/NameES` became `Names []nameInput{Lang,Field,ID,Value,Required,LabelArg}` built from `EnabledLanguages()`; the template ranges it, rendering one `name_<lang>` input per enabled language — adding a language in `/admin/org` makes a new name column appear (`TestAccountFormLanguageColumns`), and create/edit write `account_names` for each filled-in enabled language via `SetAccountName` (`TestAccountCreate/EditWritesEnabledLanguageNames`). **Stable field names/ids preserved:** `en`/`es` keep `name_en`/`name_es` and `af-name-en`/`af-name-es` (hyphenated id), so existing `accounts_test.go` and the `e2e/tests/accounts.spec.js`/`merge.spec.js` selectors (`#af-name-en`) stay green. **i18n label for an arbitrary language:** the per-language `accounts.form.name_en`/`name_es` chrome keys were replaced by ONE interpolated `accounts.form.name = "Name (%s)"` passed the uppercased code — any language gets a label without a per-language chrome key, and the UI CHROME stays en/es (`enabled_languages` is NOT wired into `i18n.Langs()`/the shell; chrome falls back to en per D14). New store read `AccountName(id,lang)` returns the EXACT per-language name (no fallback) so the edit form prefills an empty box for a language with no name yet rather than echoing the en name into a foreign input. **Admin org form** (`/admin/org`, GET+POST **Admin**, registered in `routes.go` so the permission matrix auto-covers it; linked from `admin.tmpl`): a small form (org name + enabled-languages CSV) that re-renders with a Saved notice on success (settings pages have no list to PRG to). `TestOrgSettingsPersist`/`TestOrgFormAdminOnly` + the matrix. **Tests-first (observed):** the store tests passed once the helpers existed; the web tests failed behaviorally — `/admin/org` 404 (route absent) and `name_fr` absent from the account form even with `en,es,fr` enabled (form was hardcoded en/es) — then went green after the handler/route/template refactor. `make gen` reproducible (three queries: `GetOrgSetting`/`ListOrgSettings`/`UpsertOrgSetting`); `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0; `make e2e` green (13 specs); `TestCatalogParity` green with the new `org.*` keys and the single `accounts.form.name` replacing the two `name_en/name_es` keys; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.

- **p12.2** — Transaction editor (the daily-use grid). The **five traps** are resolved as follows. (1) *Split-id round-trip:* the edit form emits each existing split's id as a hidden `split_id_<i>` field; the handler maps it into `SplitInput.ID`, so `UpdateTransaction` diffs by id — editing one split of a 3-split txn produces exactly one `splits_versions op='update'` and leaves the other two untouched (asserted via a raw `COUNT(*) FROM splits_versions`, not just latest-op). Without it, every save would delete-all + recreate-all (balances still pass, audit wrong). (2) *Pure JS:* amount parse/format, DR/CR↔signed, per-fund imbalance, fund-apply-to-all, and the keyboard-grid state machine live in `txnamount.js`/`txnfund.js`/`txngrid.js` with **no `document` access**, node-tested for real (33 cases). `txneditor.js` is the thin DOM glue (combobox/select-on-focus/date-shortcuts/gating), covered by e2e only. (3) *One DR/CR↔sign site:* the amount column posts ONE **signed** `amount_<i>` field; DR/CR twin columns are a JS convenience that normalizes into it before submit (via `drcrToSigned`), so the server is **mode-agnostic on input** — the both-modes test posts the identical form as a signed-mode and a dr_cr-mode user and gets byte-identical `splits` rows. Signed-mode entry works with no JS (`<form method=post>` degrades). (4) *Stable ids:* every input id is keyed to the row **index/split identity** (`txn-account-<i>`, `txn-splitid-<i>`, …), the SAME key that carries the split-id round-trip — a 422 re-render keeps the same ids (asserted). (5) *Server sole validator, row/totals routing:* the handler calls Post/UpdateTransaction and maps the store's typed errors to slots **without re-deriving validation** — `ErrUnbalanced`/`ErrFundUnbalanced` → the totals bar (`txn-totals-error`); row-scoped errors (`ErrAccountNotInSubsidiary`, `ErrFundProgramScope`, `ErrExpenseNeedsFunction`, `ErrNonExpenseFunction`, `Err*Program*`, inactive/missing) → the offending row (`data-row-error="<i>"`), attributed from data the editor **already loaded** (the sub-filtered account option set gives account-not-in-sub for free; a funded R/E row gives fund-program-scope; structural expense/non-expense gives the class errors). The store returns transaction-scoped errors with no split index, so attribution is a best-effort first-matching-row heuristic over the loaded options — the listed test only requires the error to land on a row, not multi-row disambiguation; an unattributable typed error falls back to the totals bar so it is never silently dropped. Two supporting reads were added (both in scope, no new dependency): `Store.GetTransaction` (live header for edit prefill) and `Store.AccountEditorOptions` (leaf+active accounts in a sub with type/default-program/default-class/subsidiary-set metadata for the combobox + client re-filter). `UserByID`'s projection was extended with `default_subsidiary_id` (mirroring p11.1's money-column extension) and `CurrentUser` gained `DefaultSubsidiaryID *int64` so the editor defaults its header subsidiary to the user's setting, else the sole/root sub. htmx success uses `HX-Redirect` (a full-page nav) so the swap never nests a register inside `#txn-form`; the subsidiary-change re-filter and the 422 error re-render both render the single-sourced `transaction-form` partial (stable ids). Scope boundary held: NO payee suggest/autofill (p12.3), void/duplicate/history (p12.4), or keyboard-only QA (p12.6) — the payee field is a plain combobox over the existing payees list. `make gen` reproducible (the one `UserByID` query change); `make lint test check` + node units + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0; `make e2e` green (16 specs incl. `txn-editor`); `TestCatalogParity` green with the new `txn.*`/`error.txn.*` keys; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
  Post-review sharpening: the header **subsidiary change re-filters server-side** (the select's hx-get re-fetches `/transactions/new?subsidiary=…` with the current rows via hx-include; the handler re-filters accounts + funds to the new sub and echoes the typed rows, flagging any row whose account left the sub — never silent-clear; no-JS friendly, the client mirrors it). Edit-prefill amounts use the **user's number format** (rule 10) so a save-without-touching round-trips (an EU-number user's "1.234,56" is emitted and re-parsed identically). The editor **currency defaults to the selected subsidiary's `base_currency`** (D18), so an MXN-subsidiary entry records in MXN rather than a hardcoded USD (the edit form overrides with the txn's stored currency). Two extra e2e specs cover the DR/CR-independent client gating: program/class selects appear only on R/E rows and prefill from the account default.
- **p12.3** — Payee autocomplete + autofill. **Four required tests, split Go/JS:** `TestPayeeSuggestRanking` (Go store) — asserts the ranked order; `TestPayeeTemplatePrefills` + `TestAutofillRespectsSubsidiary` (Go web handler) — assert the rendered partial's fields / dropped rows / notice; `TestAutofillNeverOverwrites` (JS `node --test` on the pure `allRowsEmpty`) — the client guard. **Suggest ranking (`SuggestPayees`):** active payees whose name PREFIX-matches (case-insensitive; `payees.name` is `COLLATE NOCASE`), ordered by the payee's latest NON-DELETED transaction date DESC via `LEFT JOIN transactions … AND deleted=0` grouped per payee; `ORDER BY (MAX(date) IS NULL), MAX(date) DESC, name COLLATE NOCASE, id` so **never-used or only-deleted payees rank LAST deterministically** (chosen default: unused sorts to the tail by name, not interleaved). **Active-only** suggest (a deactivated payee is not offered); recorded here as the smallest choice. **LIKE-metachar handling:** sqlc's sqlite parser REJECTS an explicit `ESCAPE` clause (and SQLite's default LIKE has no escape char), so `likePrefix` in Go neutralizes `% _ \` in the query by mapping each to the single-char wildcard `_` before appending `%` — keeps the match a true prefix (never a mid-string wildcard) for the rare payee name containing a metachar, without an escape clause. **Template (`/payees/{id}/template?sub=`):** finds the payee's last non-deleted txn (`LastTransactionForPayee`, greatest `(date,id)`), then REUSES `SplitsByTransaction` (the existing splits reader) — mapped to editor rows exactly like `txnEditForm` (account/memo/signed-amount-in-user-number-format/fund/program/class), amounts formatted in the **template txn's stored currency** (display-only prefill; the server re-validates on save). **Respects-subsidiary is SERVER-side:** splits whose account is not in the `?sub=` option set (the same `model.Accounts` the combobox offers) are DROPPED; when any drop, an i18n notice (`txn.autofill.dropped_out_of_sub`) is oob-swapped into `#txn-autofill-notice`. **Never-overwrites is CLIENT-side & pure:** `txnpayee.js` `allRowsEmpty(rows)` (no `document`) returns true only when every row has no chosen account, no typed amount/DR/CR, and no memo (a defaulted fund/program/class alone does NOT count as user intent); `txneditor.js` glue applies the fetched rows only when `allRowsEmpty` holds. **Partial reuse (no fork):** a thin `{{define "txn-rows"}}` ranges the SAME single-sourced `txn-row` template; `payee-template` wraps it + the oob notice — an autofilled row is byte-identical to a page-rendered one (stable ids / gating / wiring). **Both routes `TxnWrite`** (they feed the entry flow and exist only to author an entry, matching the editor GET forms); the permission-matrix test picks them up automatically. **Autocomplete UI (boring frontend, strict CSP):** the native `<select id=txn-payee>` stays as the no-JS **id value sink**; the JS reveals a text input (`hx-get="/payees/suggest"`, `input changed delay:150ms` → a suggestions `<ul>`) and hides the select. Picking a suggestion goes through a **delegated** click listener on the stable `#txn-payee-suggestions` container (not an `hx-*` trigger on the freshly-swapped `<li>`) and the template fetch is a **manual `fetch()`** (not htmx) — both dodge the settle-tick wiring race the task warned about. **Create-on-save (recorded interpretation, exceeds the literal build text):** a fresh `-dev` db has no payees and there is NO payee-management UI or seed hook, so the required e2e precondition ("pick a payee WITH a prior txn") can only be built in-browser by letting a saved transaction attach a NEW payee by name. `EnsurePayee(name)` find-or-creates by the NOCASE name in its OWN versioned change BEFORE the txn write (so a later txn-validation failure leaves the payee reusable, not orphaned); the editor posts the typed/picked name via a hidden `payee_name` field, and `txnSubmit` prefers a picked `payee` id else `EnsurePayee(payee_name)`. This is additive/reversible and makes the whole feature usable (an autocomplete over a permanently-empty list would be dead). No payee edit/delete/management page (not this step). **New i18n keys** (`txn.payee_search`, `txn.autofill.dropped_out_of_sub`) in BOTH catalogs — note `txn.payee.search` was renamed to `txn.payee_search` because go-i18n rejects a dotted key that turns an existing leaf (`[txn.payee]`) into a table (reserved/unreserved-key mix). `make gen` reproducible (three read queries added, ASCII, positional `?`); `make lint test check` + node units + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0; e2e green (19 specs incl. the new `payee-autofill`, run ×20 for the htmx-swap paths); `TestCatalogParity` green; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
- **p12.4** — Edit / void / duplicate + history panel. **History diff granularity — STRUCTURED in the store, RENDERED in web.** `Store.TransactionHistory(id)` returns typed `HistoryEntry{ActorID, ActorName, At, Op, HeaderDiffs, SplitDiffs}` where each `FieldDiff` carries typed old/new `DiffValue` (`Text` for date/memo/currency/functional-class, `sql.NullInt64 ID` for subsidiary/payee/account/fund/program, `int64 Amount` for money) — NOT formatted strings, because amount formatting is per-user (rule 10) and entity names are language-dependent (rule 9). The web layer (`renderHistory`) resolves ids → names in the request language, formats amounts through the money formatter honoring the user's settings, and maps each `HistoryField` to an i18n label key. This keeps the diff computation unit-testable in Go (assert old=X/new=Y, no HTML). **Diff is computed by walking consecutive snapshots per entity** (header as one entity by `entity_id`; each split by `entity_id`) then grouping the per-row diffs by `change_id` into timeline entries. Two new `:many` queries (`TransactionVersionHistory`, `SplitVersionHistory`) fetch EVERY version row (not the AsOf `LIMIT 1`) JOINed to `changes`+`users` for actor/timestamp, ordered `valid_from, id` so each entity's snapshots are consecutive; grouping re-orders into entries by **change_id ascending** (monotonic with the change timestamp: `changes.id` is autoincrement at write time, so a larger id is a later change -- this is the "ordered by the change timestamp" the audit backbone requires, and it is correct even for a SPLIT-ONLY change with no header version, e.g. an account-merge repoint, which is placed by its own change_id rather than appended after all header changes). **NULL-aware diffing is load-bearing:** reuses the store's `nullInt64Eq`/`nullStringEq` so a fund Unrestricted→set or a functional-class NULL↔set is detected — the exact deltas the step names. A `create` snapshot diffs against the empty side (initial values shown one-sided); a `delete` snapshot one-sided too; an `update` against its predecessor. An update entry's header op is ALWAYS `update` even when only a split changed (matches `UpdateTransaction`'s header-anchor), so the template renders zero header diffs rather than an empty "header changed" block. **CRITICAL void trap:** history loads from the VERSION rows by id (present regardless of the live `deleted` flag), NOT via `GetTransaction` (which returns `ErrTransactionNotFound` for a soft-deleted row) — so the history of a VOIDED txn renders (the one case it most needs); only a txn with ZERO version rows 404s. Edit and duplicate, by contrast, KEEP the live-`GetTransaction` 404 (you don't edit/duplicate a voided txn). **Void = soft-delete, not hard delete.** The route reuses `Store.DeleteTransaction` (rule 14: flip `deleted`, append ONE `transactions_versions op='delete'`, splits left live); a two-step confirm flow mirrors the merge UX — `GET /transactions/{id}/void` renders a read-only consequences review (ZERO writes), `POST` with `confirm=1` executes and redirects to `/accounts` (the txn no longer appears in any register). A `POST` without confirm falls back to the review (defensive). Both routes `TxnWrite`; a re-void of an already-voided id 404s (the review's `GetTransaction` guard). **Duplicate = editor prefilled as a NEW unsaved entry.** `GET /transactions/{id}/duplicate` (`TxnWrite`) reuses the p12.2 editor-model machinery with `TxnID=0`, `IsEdit=false`, and every row's `SplitID=""` (fresh splits inserted under a NEW txn — no diff-by-id), so the form POSTs to `/transactions` (a create). **Payee + memo are COPIED** (a duplicate is usually the same payee/purpose); **the date defaults to TODAY**, not the original's, since a duplicate is a fresh entry authored now (both defensible — the note IS the deliverable). **Timeline timestamp rendering:** rule 10 forbids `time.Format` in the render path and the money package has only a date-only `FormatDate`, so the timeline renders the change's DATE (the `changes.at` RFC3339Nano trimmed to its `YYYY-MM-DD` prefix, then through `FormatDate` in the user's format); the time-of-day is not shown (entry order disambiguates same-day edits) — a deliberate, reversible choice, not a rule-10 violation (parsing the machine timestamp with the string prefix is fine). **Entry points:** the register row (`register.tmpl`) gains an always-present Actions cell with plain full-page `<a>` links (edit / duplicate / void / history) — plain nav keeps the CSP trivial and avoids the htmx-settle dance (only the editor's own JS is reused, unchanged); `regColspan` bumped 7→8 (the register colspan/thead tests picked it up). **Perm enforcement asserted explicitly** (beyond the auto matrix): `TestVoidRequiresConfirmAndTxnWrite` proves a `read` user gets 403 on GET+POST void while the txn stays live, then a `write` user's confirm voids it; `TestHistoryTxnReadMayView` proves `read` may view history. **i18n:** new `history.*`, `void.*`, `register.action.*`, `register.col.actions` keys in BOTH catalogs (`history.split.line` is a `tn` plural); watched the dotted-key/leaf collision (no bare `history` leaf beside `history.*`). `make gen` reproducible (two ASCII positional-`?` `:many` queries added); `make lint test check` + node units + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0; `make e2e` green (22 specs incl. the new `txn-history`, validated ×20 for the swap-touching path); `TestCatalogParity` + the auto permission-matrix green with the four new routes; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
- **p12.5** — Funds workspace (`/funds` list + `/funds/{id}` statement + create/edit/close/reopen). **Negative-badge sign rule (Z18):** the list's warning badge is `FundBalancesAsOf(fund) < 0` per currency (net-debit, D2: a fund's ASSET-side sum going negative = overspent restricted resources). This is NOT a fresh computation — it reuses the p08.4 `FundBalancesAsOf` query, which already sums ONLY asset splits (a sum over ALL a fund's splits is identically 0 by fund conservation, D20/Z10). The badge fires if ANY currency is negative (BecaAgua carries both MXN and USD; the fixture deliberately keeps every fund non-negative, so the negative-badge Go test builds an overspent fund inline — receive 500, spend 900, each txn fund-balanced → asset cash −400). **Fund-ledger opening-balance computation:** the statement is a new `FundLedger(fund_id, asof)` query — every non-deleted split tagged the fund whose txn date ≤ asof, across ALL accounts, ordered `(date, split_id)`, with a per-currency RUNNING BALANCE whose window sums ONLY asset splits (`CASE WHEN a.type='asset' THEN sp.amount ELSE 0 END` inside `SUM() OVER (PARTITION BY currency ORDER BY date, id)`). So the running balance tracks the fund's UNEXPENDED (asset-side) position — the SAME quantity the list shows and Z18 warns on — and the CLOSING running balance per currency EQUALS `FundBalancesAsOf(asof)` by construction. **The statement uses the SAME as-of the list uses** (`s.now()`, i.e. today): binding both pages to one as-of makes them agree on a fund's closing balance EVEN under FUTURE-dated splits (a post-dated payment) — without the bound they'd silently disagree, since the list is date-bounded (`FundBalancesAsOf` filters `t.date <= today`) while an unbounded ledger would sum splits dated after today. `TestFundLedgerAsOfMatchesFundBalances` posts a 2099-dated fund split and asserts reconciliation at three as-ofs (past, mid, future) to lock the agreement. **Opening is 0** (the whole set to the as-of is shown from the fund's first split; there is NO period filter — the task doesn't require one, and a fund's splits already live only in its subsidiaries, so no scope filter either). This reconciliation (`closing == FundBalancesAsOf(asof) == list balance`) is the coherence invariant, asserted directly in `TestFundLedger` (store), `TestFundLedgerAsOfMatchesFundBalances` (store, future-dated), and `TestFundStatementOpeningClosing` (web). Non-asset rows (revenue/expense) are STILL SHOWN (per "splits across all accounts") but render "—" in the running column and leave the balance unchanged. **Closed-fund toggle semantics:** `CloseFund` sets `active=0` (p07.3, op=update, audited — never a delete, rule 14); the list splits on `active` via `?closed=1`, showing exactly the active OR the closed set (never both). Close/reopen are inline POST ACTIONS (mirroring `programDeactivate`), NOT a form — the subsidiary checklist + program scope belong to create/edit only. `fundClose` redirects to `/funds?closed=1` (you just closed it, so land where it now lives); `fundReopen` to `/funds`. **Program-scope handling:** the create/edit form has an OPTIONAL program-scope `<select>` (a fund scopes to ≥1 subsidiary via the `sub_<id>` checklist reusing the accounts pattern, D20, and OPTIONALLY a program subtree). On UPDATE, `program_id` is ALWAYS sent as a non-nil pointer (0 = clear, positive = set) using the store's non-nil-0-clears convention; the subsidiary checklist is passed as a NON-NIL slice (`nonNilSubs`) so an empty checklist is treated as "desired = empty" → `ErrFundNoSubsidiary` (rather than nil = "leave unchanged"). **Perms:** fund grants are BOOKKEEPING data (D20, managed like programs), so GET list+statement = TxnRead, create/edit/close/reopen = TxnWrite (subsidiaries/users stay Admin — unchanged). `TestFundsPermReadCannotManage` asserts (beyond the auto matrix) that a `read` user views `/funds` + a statement (200) but is 403 on POST create, POST close, and GET `/funds/new`. **Required assertions, split Go/node:** all funds assertions are Go (store `TestFundLedger`/`TestFundLedgerExcludesOtherFunds`; web list/statement/form/perm) — this step adds NO client logic (the closed toggle is a plain `?closed=1` link; the form uses only htmx attributes), so NO new node-tested module. A new store read `FundSubsidiaryIDs` (mirrors `AccountSubsidiaryIDs`) feeds the list's scope column + the edit form's checklist pre-check. **Matrix seed:** `routes_test.go` now seeds one fund so `/funds/{id}` + `/funds/{id}/edit` resolve for the reachability check (the same pattern the account/txn seeds use). **i18n:** new `funds.*`/`error.fund.*` keys in BOTH catalogs — watched the dotted-key/leaf collision (renamed the statement-button leaf `funds.statement` → `funds.view_statement` because `[funds.statement]` collides with `[funds.statement.title]` etc.). `make gen` reproducible (one ASCII positional-`?` `:many` query added, `FundLedger`); `make lint test check` + node units + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0; `make e2e` green (23 specs incl. the new `funds` spec covering create-with-checklist+program → statement → close → reopen, validated ×20 with 4 parallel workers, no flake); `TestCatalogParity` + the auto permission-matrix green with the eight new routes; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged.
- **p12.6** — Entry-flow hardening + the manual QA script `docs/qa-entry.md` (focus retention, zero layout shift, scroll preservation, keyboard-only 4-split mixed-fund entry, es locale pass). **Automated the two Tests bullets at the handler layer** (no store mocks, real router): `TestTxnStableInputIDsAcrossAllSwaps` extends the existing p12.2 `TestTxnStableInputIDsAcrossRerender` to assert row-0 input ids survive **every** in-flow swap — the subsidiary re-filter `hx-get` swap **and** an htmx 422 re-render, not only the non-htmx 422; `TestTxnInFlowActionsNeverFullReload` proves in-flow editor actions never full-reload mid-entry — the re-filter and 422 swaps return the `#txn-form` **partial** (no doctype/`<html>`/`<nav>`), while a successful save returns **HX-Redirect** to the first split's register (the ONE intentional navigation) and does **not** swap the editor back in. Added a test-only `asHTMXUser` helper (asUser + the `HX-Request` header) + an `isFullPage` body check. **Keyboard-only e2e** (`e2e/tests/entry-keyboard.spec.js`) drives a real 4-split mixed-fund entry with `page.keyboard` events only (Tab/Shift+Tab, Arrow-driven native `<select>` operation via a deterministic `selectByKeyboard` helper — no `selectOption`, the Add-row `<button>` activated by Enter, typed amounts, the date `t` shortcut); the 4 splits balance per-fund (D20: Water Grant +40−40, Unrestricted +10−10) so it is a genuine mixed-fund post. The spec also Tab-walks an asset row's tail (fund → memo) and asserts focus lands on `#txn-memo-0`, **proving** the hidden program/class cells are skipped by native Tab. Stable ×20 solo + ×21 in the full parallel suite (the DoD's ~20× parallel gate), zero flakes. **FINDING (documented + flagged, deliberately NOT fixed here):** `txngrid.js`'s pure `nextCell` grid state machine (Enter-advance, Alt+Arrow row-move, Ctrl/Cmd+Enter save, Escape cancel, Enter-add-row-on-last-cell) is node-tested and **imported** by the DOM glue `txneditor.js` but **never called** — no `keydown` listener consults it — so those keys are inert in the browser today. Keyboard entry is **not broken**: native Tab + native select keyboard ops + the Add-row button cover a full 4-split entry (proven by the spec), and hidden program/class cells (`visibility:hidden`) are correctly skipped by native Tab. Per the p12.6 posture ("do NOT refactor unless it genuinely breaks keyboard entry — flag before a big refactor") this is a **missing ergonomic enhancement**, not a hardening fix: correct wiring would need a skip-hidden traversal (`nextCell` moves col+1 blindly and would land focus on the hidden program/class cells) that does not exist and is untested — i.e. p12.2-scoped feature work left for the orchestrator to green-light. **p12.2 settle-wiring follow-up CONFIRMED:** it does not bite keyboard entry — the account form's self-swapping type select is not in the editor; the editor's only swapped-in `hx-*` triggers are the subsidiary re-filter (set once, before typing rows) and the payee suggest input, and the payee template fetch is fired via a **manual `fetch`** (not an `hx-*` trigger on a freshly-swapped node — `fetchAndApplyTemplate`), so nothing races the settle tick; no account-form refactor. **No i18n/schema/query changes** (all `txn.*`/`error.txn.*` keys already exist in both catalogs). **es locale pass OBSERVED, not inferred:** `TestTxnEditorEsNoRawKeys` sets the user's `locale='es'` (D14: a logged-in user's stored locale is authoritative over `?lang=`, so `?lang=es` does NOT switch an authenticated user's UI — corrected in qa-entry.md) and GETs the editor, asserting the es column headers/title/apply-all button render, that the en title does NOT leak (no fallback-to-en), and that no raw `txn.`/`error.txn.` key substring appears. `make lint test check` + node units green; `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the persistent informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding only); `make e2e` full parallel suite green (24 test cases across 13 spec files, incl. the new `entry-keyboard` spec).
- **p12.6 keyboard grid wiring** (follow-up to the FINDING above, user green-lit) — RESOLVED the "`nextCell` imported but never called" gap. **Pure layer (`txngrid.js`, node-tested):** `nextCell` gained a sixth param `isVisible(row, col) -> bool` (default `() => true`, so every prior test/behavior is byte-identical). `advance`/`retreat` became scanning loops that step forward/backward one cell at a time and **skip** cells where `isVisible` is false until they hit a visible cell or a grid boundary; each step strictly increases (forward) / decreases (backward) the position, so the scan provably terminates even on a fully-hidden row (guarded by a node test). Enter's add-row is now driven off advance's boundary result ("no visible cell forward on the last row") rather than a literal `col === cols-1`, so it stays correct even when trailing columns are hidden. New node tests cover: forward-skip over hidden program/class (fund→memo), backward-skip (memo→fund), Enter add-row at the last **visible** cell (incl. a trailing-hidden grid), Alt+Arrow unaffected by visibility, and the fully-hidden-row no-loop. **Column model:** the editable cells, in DOM/tab order, are mode-dependent — signed mode `account, amount, fund, program, class, memo` (6 cols); DR/CR mode `account, dr, cr, fund, program, class, memo` (7 cols, the amount split into two visible columns). The hidden `split_id` sink, the DR/CR-mode hidden signed `amount` sink, and the row-error `<td>` are **not** focus columns. `program` is visible iff the row's account type ∈ {revenue, expense}; `class` iff expense — the SAME `rowReveal` decision `gateRow` uses to toggle `visibility` (single source of truth, no duplication). **DOM glue (`txneditor.js`, e2e-covered):** a `keydown` handler is attached to `.txn-grid` (NOT the form) — structurally scoped, because the payee autocomplete and date inputs live in `.txn-header` **outside** the table, so the grid handler can never fight their existing keydown handlers. It parses the focused input's stable id (`txn-<field>-<i>`) → `{row, col}` via the column model (ids never move, so this is the focus↔cell bridge), builds `isVisible` from `rowReveal`, calls `nextCell` with `mods.ctrl = ctrlKey || metaKey` (Cmd≡Ctrl per the module header), and dispatches: `move`→focus the target input (but at a boundary where target==current it does **not** preventDefault, so native Tab carries focus out to the Save/Add-row controls — no focus trap); `add-row`→existing `addRow()` then focus the new row's first cell; `save`→`form.requestSubmit(submitBtn)` (fires htmx + native validation, unlike `form.submit()`); `cancel`→click the Cancel `<a>`; `move-row-up/down`→swap the two rows' field **values** (ids stay stable) then re-gate/recompute and follow focus. Enter is intercepted (preventDefault on move/add-row) so it never leaks a stray native form submit. **e2e (`entry-keyboard.spec.js`):** a second test drives the wired shortcuts with real `page.keyboard` — Enter advances account→amount→fund→**memo** on an asset row (asserting focus never lands on `#txn-program-0`/`#txn-class-0`), Shift+Tab/Tab prove the same skip backward/forward, Alt+ArrowDown reorders two rows (values swap, focus follows), and Ctrl+Enter from a mid-grid cell saves (HX-Redirect to the register). Stable across 20× parallel repeats of the keyboard spec (`--repeat-each=20 --workers=4`, 40 executions) + 20× full-suite parallel runs (`--workers=4`), zero flakes. Note (UX call for the orchestrator): Escape-as-cancel is wired per the task. Empirically probed (Chromium): Escape while a native `<select>` **popup is open** stays on the editor — the popup swallows the key so the grid handler never fires (no data loss on that path); Escape only cancels when a grid **text input** is focused (the intended Appendix C behavior). It still navigates away from a half-entered grid with no confirm — revisit if that feels too abrupt. DR/CR (7-col) column mapping is verified by inspection against the template cell order only — node tests use abstract grids and the e2e runs in the default signed mode — so DR/CR keyboard traversal is not test-covered.

- **p13.1** — **My settings** (`/settings`, AnyUser): the personal-preferences page consolidating language, date/number formats, display mode (signed vs DR/CR), negative style, theme, and default subsidiary into ONE versioned write. **No schema change** — the p06.1 migration already added every column (`locale`, `date_format`, `number_format`, `display_mode`, `neg_style`, `theme`, `default_subsidiary_id`) with a `users_versions` twin, and format.go already maps them per-user; p13.1 only PERSISTS them. **Versioned update:** new sqlc `UpdateUserSettings` is the LIVE update ONLY (positional `?`, ASCII); the store method reuses the existing snapshot-from-live `InsertUserVersion` inside one `write(ctx,"user.settings",...)` so the op=update snapshot captures all seven columns naming the actor (matches `SetUserTheme`). `cuento check` stays clean. **Validation set (the store is the guard — the migration puts a CHECK only on `txn_perm`, so these columns have NO DB backstop):** `date_format` ∈ ISO/US/EU; `number_format` ∈ US/EU/plain; `display_mode` ∈ signed/dr_cr; `neg_style` ∈ minus/parens; `theme` ∈ auto/light/dark (reused `ValidTheme`); `locale` via an injected `localeOK` closure (the web layer passes `known`/`i18n.Langs`, keeping the store i18n-free). Any unknown → `ErrInvalidSetting` BEFORE the funnel opens (so a reject writes no version row). **Default-subsidiary clearing:** nullable — an empty form value clears it to NULL; a non-empty id is existence-checked in-store (`GetSubsidiary`) so a bad id is a clean 422, not an FK-triggered 500. **Form convention:** a FULL-PAGE form (like `/admin/org`, not an inline htmx swap): success → 303 PRG to `/settings?saved=1` so the new locale/theme render on the fresh GET; invalid (only reachable by a crafted POST past the fixed `<select>`s) → whole page re-rendered at 422 with the p10.3 `formErrors`+autofocus adapted to a full page (no partial region to swap). **Theme cookie on save:** `resolveTheme` reads the `cuento_theme` cookie BEFORE the DB, so the POST also re-sets the cookie (exactly like `setTheme`) or the next render would show the stale cookie theme; locale needs no such step (`resolveLang` reads the DB for logged-in users). The header theme control (POST /theme) and login language switcher are UNCHANGED (shell.spec relies on them). **AUDIT (the "all render paths through p03 formatters + {{t}}" clause) — clean, nothing to fix:** grepped web handlers + templates for `time.Format`/`strconv`/`.Format`/raw amounts and hardcoded English. Every raw `.Format("2006-01-02")` produces the ISO-CANONICAL string the store consumes (as-of dates, cursors, query params) — NOT display; every user-facing date goes through `money.FormatDate(_, dateFormatFor(u))` (accounts `AsOf`, programs `From`/`To`, register/fund rows) and every amount through `money.Format` into pre-formatted `string` model fields; user-facing text is `{{t}}`. Only the `-dev` styleguide has literal color-swatch names (a component gallery, never production, not app content). **Tests:** `TestFormatsFollowUserSettings` posts one 1,234.50 debit dated 2025-03-15 and GETs the SAME register as two read users through the real router — user A (US/ISO/signed) body has `1,234.50`+`2025-03-15`+no DR/CR; user B (EU/EU/dr_cr) body has `1.234,50`+`15/03/2025`+a DR/CR marker and NOT `1,234.50`, plus `bodyA != bodyB`. `TestLocaleSwitchSwapsChrome` renders /settings for an es user and asserts es strings in BOTH the sliced `app-nav` (Ajustes/Cuentas) and `<main>` (Idioma/Formato de fecha/Tema), `lang="es"`, and that raw keys (`nav.settings`, `settings.language`, …) do NOT leak. Store tests assert the versioned round-trip (actor named, default-sub set then cleared) and per-field rejection (no version row on reject). e2e `settings.spec.js` switches locale→es + display→dr_cr, saves (full-page 303 to a DIFFERENT URL → `waitForURL(**/settings?**)`, never the no-op same-url pattern; no `waitForFunction` under the strict CSP), and asserts the es chrome on a subsequent /accounts page. Stable 20x under `--repeat-each=20 --workers=4`.
 **e2e worker-scoped isolation:** the `server` fixture is WORKER-scoped (one db shared across a worker's tests), so unlike the theme (a per-context cookie) a durable locale change to the SHARED admin poisons sibling tests in the same worker (txn-editor's English "New account" selector fails when the admin is left in es). settings.spec therefore RESTORES the admin to the seeded defaults (en/signed) before finishing; verified 5x full-suite green (26 specs) + 20x settings.spec parallel.
 The restore uses value-based/language-independent selectors (selectOption + `form.settings-form button[type="submit"]`, never a label regex) so a mid-test failure cannot cascade es-selector confusion; NO other spec file was modified (the txn-editor flake was purely this poisoning, not a latent race).

- **p13.2 (web: admin)** — The admin surface (`/admin/**`, all Admin perm) adds users management, per-user permissions, and currencies; the `/admin` stub becomes a real section index linking users/subsidiaries/currencies/org (org settings reuse p11.4 unchanged). Non-obvious calls:
  - **txn_perm enum = `none`/`read`/`write`** (the migration 00006 CHECK). The new versioned `SetUserTxnPerm` validates against this set (`store.ErrInvalidTxnPerm`) BEFORE the write — the column CHECK is only a backstop, mirroring the p13.1 settings validators. The web select offers exactly these three; the store is the guard.
  - **Last-admin guard keys on OTHER-enabled-admin count, not `CountHumanUsers`.** `CountHumanUsers` is `WHERE id<>1` (a non-system count) — using it would let "5 viewers + 1 admin" pass and lock out all admin access. `DisableUser` now loads the target and, if it is an admin, counts ENABLED admins OTHER than it (`CountOtherEnabledAdmins`); zero → `ErrLastAdmin`. The system user (id 1) can never be disabled (`ErrSystemUser`). The guard lives in the STORE so both the web handler AND the CLI `user disable` honor it (the CLI only ever disables non-admins in its tests, so unaffected). The web maps `ErrLastAdmin` to a page-level 422 (the guard is shown, nothing executed — like subsidiaries' `ErrHasActiveChildren`).
  - **System user (id 1) is unmanageable → detail routes REDIRECT to the list.** `TestRouteRegistryComplete` substitutes `{id}`→1 for parameterized routes; id 1 is the seeded system user, which the store's `AdminUserByID`/`SetUserTxnPerm`/grant writers refuse (`ErrSystemUser`). Returning 404 for id 1 would fail reachability ("not mounted"). So `GET /admin/users/{id}`, `POST .../txn-perm`, and `POST .../grants` map `ErrSystemUser` to a **303 → /admin/users** (it exists but is off-limits; a 303 is non-404 and non-login-302, so both the matrix and reachability tests pass), while a genuinely-unknown id stays a **404** (`ErrUserNotFound`; reachability never substitutes an unknown id). disable/reset also redirect the system user to the list, so all five treat it uniformly. This preserves rule 8 (routes auto-included from the registry) without special-casing the test.
  - **Currency management is NOT versioned** — `currencies` is static reference data (D1), absent from Appendix A's versions list and from the `cuento check` Z5 union (no `currencies_versions` twin). So `AddCurrency`/`SetCurrencyActive` are plain reference-data writes OUTSIDE the write funnel (no actor, no `changes` row), exactly like `SyncReportGroups`/`SetOrgSetting`. `AddCurrency` is an idempotent UPSERT (a re-add refreshes metadata + re-enables) so an admin re-adding an existing code — or a same-worker e2e retry — never PK-collides. Shape (3 uppercase letters, exponent 0..4, non-empty symbol/name) is validated in the store (`ErrInvalidCurrency`); the handler uppercases the code first.
  - **Grant model = composite-key versioned set, mirroring account_subsidiaries.** `user_report_grants_versions` keys `entity_id = user_id` with `group_name` as a snapshot column and part of the identity. `GrantReportGroup` guards with `HasReportGrant` (a re-grant is a no-op, no duplicate PK / no spurious version row), inserts live, then snapshots op='create'; `RevokeReportGroup` INVERTS the order — snapshot op='delete' BEFORE the live delete (the row must still exist to snapshot). The per-user page submits the FULL desired checkbox set; the handler diffs against current grants and issues one versioned grant per added group + one versioned revoke per removed group. Each perm/grant change is one `changes` row naming the acting admin (`store.Actor` from context) — precisely what `TestPermChangeVersioned` asserts: it uses `AssertVersioned`/`AssertVersionedGrant` for op + change existence, then `LatestVersionActor`/`LatestGrantActor` for the actor (the op helpers deliberately do not check `actor_id`), over a grant→revoke→re-grant round trip (create→delete→create).
  - **Password create/reset reuse `internal/auth.Hash` (argon2id, rule 13)** — the same credential path login uses; never hand-rolled. Users are never deleted (disable only). A duplicate username surfaces as `store.ErrUsernameTaken` (typed from the UNIQUE constraint) → a 422 username field error, not a 500.
  - **e2e isolation:** `admin.spec.js` logs in as the shared `e2eadmin` but creates and mutates its OWN uniquely-named user and adds a currency with a UNIQUE random 3-letter code, so nothing durable leaks into sibling specs on the worker-scoped shared db. Language-independent selectors (ids, form selectors, `data-username`/`data-code` row attributes); no `waitForFunction` (strict CSP). Full parallel suite verified 20× green, zero flakes.
- **p14.1 (db+store: rates)** — `exchange_rates(rate_date, base, quote, rate REAL, source, change_id, PK(rate_date, base, quote))` (migration `00013`), FKs base/quote→`currencies(code)` and change_id→`changes(id)`, plus index `(base, quote, rate_date)` for the on-or-before lookup. Non-obvious calls:
  - **`exchange_rates` is CHANGE-ID-ANCHORED, NOT versioned.** A rate is a fact about a day, not an editable entity with a reconstructable history, so there is no `exchange_rates_versions` twin, no trigger, no snapshot-from-live append — it is absent from Appendix A's versions list and from the `cuento check` Z5 union (like `currencies`/`report_groups`/`org_settings`). But UNLIKE those pure-reference tables, a rate load IS audited: `PutRates` runs through the store write funnel so a whole batch shares ONE `changes` row, recorded directly in `change_id` (who loaded these rates, when). **Z-invariant awareness: NONE needed** — this is the deliberate design decision the step flagged. Z5 checks `versions → changes` only; NO check asserts the reverse (`changes → some version`), because reference-data writes bypass the funnel entirely and even p06.1's system-user backfill only added a version row to keep Z5 clean, never a changes-coverage rule. So a rates-only `changes` row (referenced by no `*_versions` row) trips nothing. Proven empirically by `TestExtendRatesKeepsLedgerClean`: after `ExtendRates` loads 18 audited rate rows, `ledger.Check` still returns 0 Errors + exactly the fixture's 1 Z19 warning. `make check` (fresh migrated empty db, no rates) stays clean.
  - **`RateOn(base, quote, date) (store.RateResult, error)`** where `RateResult{Rate float64, RateDate string, Reciprocal bool}`. Resolution order: (1) `base == quote` → identity `1.0` with `RateDate = date`, **no row needed** (an identity rate is never stale, so the date is immaterial to footnotes); (2) a **DIRECT** `(base,quote)` row with the greatest `rate_date <= date` (`RateOnOrBefore` = `ORDER BY rate_date DESC LIMIT 1`) — direct **always wins**, even over a later reciprocal, because only a genuine `sql.ErrNoRows` falls through; (3) else a **RECIPROCAL** `(quote,base)` row on-or-before (same query, swapped args) → `1/rate` with `Reciprocal=true` and the inverse row's ACTUAL date; (4) else `ErrRateMissing`, wrapped with `%w` so p15 callers `errors.Is` it to footnote a conversion gap rather than fail. **Staleness:** `RateOn` returns the row's REAL `rate_date`, never echoes the query `date`, so a report says "as of <rate_date>" when the newest rate predates the query (`TestRateStaleness`).
  - **`PutRates(ctx, []store.Rate)` = "batch, one change".** Every row of a batch is inserted in a loop inside a SINGLE `s.write(ctx, "rates.put", …)` call, so all rows share the funnel's one `change_id` (`TestPutRatesOneChange` asserts `COUNT(DISTINCT change_id) == 1` across the batch and that a second batch is a distinct change). An empty batch is a no-op — no rate rows AND no `changes` row (nothing to audit; `TestPutRatesEmptyNoChange`). `InsertRate` is an idempotent UPSERT on the PK so a ratesync retry / manual correction over the same day+pair overwrites (refreshing rate/source and re-anchoring `change_id` to the loading batch) rather than PK-colliding. `rate` is a `REAL`/`float64` per the PLAN spec and D12 (the only place float64 is allowed, rule 3); conversion/rounding is p15's, not here — inserts are plain positional `?` (no `INSERT…SELECT`, so the p04.2 numbered-param quirk does not apply); `rates.sql` kept pure ASCII.
  - **Fixture seam `ExtendRates` (p14 seam filled).** Loads **18 monthly USD→MXN points** 2025-01-01 (17.00) → 2026-06-01 (18.10) via `PutRates` (one audited batch, source `"fixture"`), spanning the fixture's transaction range.
