The i-th rate is the EXACT linear interpolation `17.00 + i*(18.10-17.00)/17` — a fixed, re-computable formula (no clock/network). **OPT-IN:** `New` does NOT call `ExtendRates`, so the default fixture stays native-currency and every existing native-currency expectation is untouched; `f.Expected.Rates` is the zero value until a p15 test opts in. **Converted expectations are UNROUNDED floats** (`RatesExpected.ConvertedFundBalances`): p15 owns the rounding mode + rules (D12), so pinning rounded int64 here would pre-commit p15 to reproduce this step's arithmetic. The documented conversion RULE p15 must conform to: report base USD; an MXN balance converts at the **CLOSING** rate on-or-before AsOf (2026-06-30 → the 2026-06-01 point, 18.10) via the reciprocal `1/18.10` (`RateOn(MXN,USD,AsOf)`); USD funds pass through 1:1. `TestExtendRatesConvertedFundBalances` checks the derivation is internally consistent with the native `FundBalances`.
- **p14.2 (tools: ratesync + CSV import)** — The two rate-loading paths (auto-fetch + manual backfill) over p14.1's `PutRates`. Non-obvious calls:
  - **`RateSource` seam isolates the FRAGILE Yahoo dependency (new package `internal/rates`).** Yahoo Finance's chart endpoint is UNOFFICIAL and WILL break someday, so `cuento ratesync` depends only on `rates.RateSource` (`Fetch(ctx, []rates.Pair) ([]store.Rate, error)`); the Yahoo implementation lives behind it in `internal/rates/yahoo.go` (`Yahoo{BaseURL, Client}` + `NewYahoo()` with a 15s timeout). The blast radius of a Yahoo shape change is one file + one parser, never the command/store/tests.
  - **The PARSER is the tested unit; NO network in `go test` (AGENTS testing convention + DATA RULE 11).** `parseYahoo(pair, body) → store.Rate` is exercised entirely against SYNTHETIC, hand-authored bodies in `internal/rates/testdata/` (`yahoo_usdmxn.json`, `yahoo_empty.json`, `yahoo_error.json`) — NOT real captured payloads. `TestYahooParse` asserts the right (base, quote, value) AND that `rate_date` is DERIVED from the body's `regularMarketTime` (Unix seconds) rendered in **UTC** (`time.Unix(t,0).UTC().Format("2006-01-02")`), never the machine clock — the recorded `1704067200` → `2024-01-01`. Defensive because the endpoint is unofficial: empty result / Yahoo error channel / missing price → typed `ErrNoData` (not a panic, not a zero rate); malformed JSON → a wrapped decode error (`TestYahooParse{Empty,Error,Malformed,MissingPrice}`). Pointers on `regularMarketPrice`/`regularMarketTime` distinguish "field absent" from a real 0. The HTTP shim is thin (`BaseURL` settable so a test could point at a local server; a per-pair `ErrNoData` is SKIPPED so one delisted symbol never sinks the batch, but a transport/non-200 error aborts the whole fetch).
  - **CONFIGURED PAIRS = ACTIVE currencies × the ORG BASE, identity skipped (zero-config, derived — NOT an org-settings key).** `ratesyncPairs` takes the org base from the ROOT subsidiary's `base_currency` (`SubTree(ctx)[0]`, pre-order so the root is first; empty tree → a clear error, no index panic) — because report base currency FOLLOWS the scoped subsidiary (D18), it is INTENTIONALLY not an `org_settings` key (see `org_settings.go`). Pairs = `{(base, c) : c ∈ active currencies, c ≠ base}`, direction base→quote matching Yahoo's `USDMXN=X` symbol build and `exchange_rates`'s base→quote multiplier. Adding an active currency auto-extends coverage; nothing to maintain (`TestRatesyncPairsFromCurrencies`).
  - **`cuento ratesync` (`cmd/cuento/ratesync.go`, wired in `main.go` dispatch + usage).** Same open-the-db convention as the other subcommands (`openStore`, `-db` flag). `runRatesync(ctx, st, src)` derives the pairs, does ONE `Fetch`, and `PutRates` the whole batch as ONE change under the system actor (`store.WithActor(ctx, systemActor)` bound INSIDE the func, mirroring `user.go`, so a source error writes NOTHING — `TestRatesyncSourceErrorNoWrite` proves the no-partial-write; `TestRatesyncWritesFetched` proves the happy path via `RateOn`). No network in any test (a `fakeSource` injects canned results). **The systemd timer that runs this unattended is documented in phase 18 (p18), NOT built here** — only referenced.
  - **Admin CSV upload (`/admin/rates`, Perm Admin) — the FIRST multipart upload in the app.** `ratesImport` uses stdlib `r.ParseMultipartForm`/`r.FormFile` (1 MiB cap) + `encoding/csv`. **All-or-nothing:** `parseRatesCSV` validates the exact header `rate_date,base,quote,rate,source` and EVERY row (`FieldsPerRecord`=5; `rate_date` strict `YYYY-MM-DD`; base/quote uppercased + known-currency check; `rate` a positive float; non-empty `source`) and builds the FULL `[]store.Rate` batch BEFORE any write — the first bad thing returns a `csvError{key, arg}` (i18n key + offending line number) and `PutRates` is never called, so a partial import can't leave the books half-loaded (`TestRatesCSVImport`: a valid file imports N rows verified via `RateOn`; a bad header AND a bad data row after a valid one each 422 with nothing written). `PutRates` runs under `s.actorCtx(r.Context())` (the funnel needs the acting admin; the batch is one change). Reuses the form-error convention as a **page-level 422** (a file input can't be echoed back on re-render, so no inline partial swap — same shape as the currencies add-error). New i18n keys `admin.rates.*` in BOTH catalogs (`imported` is a `tn` plural; `admin.rates`/`admin.rates.error` are prefixes only, no leaf/prefix collision). The matrix test picked up the two new `/admin/rates` routes automatically (rule 8).
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `net/http`/`encoding/csv`/`encoding/json`/`mime/multipart` only); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. **e2e** `e2e/tests/rates-import.spec.js`: an admin adds two OWN uniquely-coded currencies then uploads a rates CSV between them on a random far-future date (worker-scoped-db isolation — nothing shared is touched) via `setInputFiles` with an in-memory Buffer, and sees the imported-count confirmation; a bad-header upload shows the error, not a crash. `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); the full parallel e2e suite (28 specs) green 20×.
- **p15.1 (reports: framework)** — The report FRAMEWORK every Phase-15 report (p15.3–p15.11) plugs into: a report SHAPE + the machine renderer in a new `internal/reports` package (no HTTP, no html/template — so it never imports `web`, avoiding a `reports→web→reports` cycle), and the generic HTTP/HTML glue in `web`. Non-obvious calls:
  - **Report SHAPE = pure data + a Run func:** `reports.Report{ID, TitleKey, Group, ParamsSpec, Run(ctx, *Toolkit, Params) (Table, error)}`. `ID` is the URL slug + registry key (lowercase ascii/digits/-/_, unique); `TitleKey` an i18n message id (rule 9 — the package renders NO text); `Group` a permission bucket; `ParamsSpec` declares which shared params the report consumes; `Run` is a pure read (rule 2, no funnel). The `Registry` (`reports.NewRegistry`/`Default`) is iterable and PANICS on a malformed registration (empty/bad id, dup id, empty title, undeclared group, nil Run) — a build-time defect surfaced at startup like `mustParseTemplates`, never at request time. `reports.Default()` assembles the shipped set (today: the smoke report); p15.3+ each add one `reg.Register(...)` line and nothing else changes.
  - **The report-GROUP set (replaces the p06.3 `_placeholder`):** `reports.Groups() = {financial, funds, programs, tax}` — small, aligned to the Phase-15 categories by AUDIENCE/permission need (financial statements p15.3–6+9; funds p15.8; programs p15.10; IRS-990/tax p15.7+11), NOT by data source, so an org can grant a bookkeeper the statements without the 990 package. `web.codeReportGroups()` now returns `reports.Groups()` (the web layer still owns the sync because route Perms reference the names); `SyncReportGroups` upserts ALL declared names, so a group can exist before any report references it. p13.2's admin grant UI now shows the real four (raw names, no i18n — the grant checkbox renders `.Name` verbatim, confirmed). `routes_test.go`'s `placeholderReportGroup` constant → `grantedReportGroup = "financial"` (the smoke report's group) and the ReportsOnly persona is granted it — so the existing `TestPermissionMatrix` proves granted→200/ungranted→403 on the real report route with ZERO new matrix code.
  - **Routes auto-mount CONCRETE per report, not a `/reports/{id}` wildcard (the load-bearing routing choice):** `routes()` iterates `s.reports.All()` and appends a literal `Route{GET, "/reports/"+id, ReportGroup(group), reportPage}` AND `"/reports/"+id+".csv"` per report. Concrete (not wildcard) because (a) each report needs its OWN group Perm, which one wildcard route can't carry; (b) `routes_test.go`'s `concreteURL` substitutes `{seg}→"1"`, so a wildcard `/reports/{id}` would resolve to bogus id `1` and 404 the completeness check; (c) an unknown `/reports/{id}` then simply never matches a route and the mux 404s on its own (rule 8: the whole surface is these declared routes). Because the routes are appended to the SAME registry the matrix iterates, every report route is permission-tested automatically (the "appears in the matrix" requirement). The handler derives WHICH report from the request path (last segment minus `.csv`), since concrete routes carry no `{id}` PathValue.
  - **Table = typed cells, rendered by BOTH a generic HTML template and the CSV writer:** `reports.Table{Columns[], Rows[]}`; a `Cell` is `CellText` (a stored proper noun rendered VERBATIM) / `CellLabel` (an i18n message KEY the renderers localize) / `CellMoney` (int64 minor + ISO currency, rule 3 — EXACT, never pre-formatted) / `CellDate` (ISO string); a `Row` carries `Indent` (tree depth), a `RowKind` (`RowData/RowSubtotal/RowTotal/RowWarning`), where `RowWarning` is the D19 intercompany net-nonzero row (rendered `role="alert"`, never dropped). **The label/proper-noun distinction is EXPLICIT at the cell kind (`TextCell` vs `LabelCell`), NOT guessed from the string** — a deliberate foundation choice (advisor-flagged): nine reports (p15.3–11) inherit it, and a 990-preparer report must never render a raw i18n key nor wrongly translate an account name. `renderCell` (HTML) localizes `CellLabel` via `i18n.T`, renders `CellText` verbatim, and formats money/date per the user's settings (rule 10); the CSV path resolves `CellLabel→CellText` once (`localizeLabelCells`) before the i18n-free `WriteCSV`. ONE generic `report.tmpl` renders any Table, so p15.3+ never touch a template or the handler.
  - **CSV = stdlib `encoding/csv`, machine-plain + correctly escaped:** `reports.WriteCSV(w, table, localize, exps)` uses `csv.Writer` (RFC 4180 quoting), money in `NumberPlain` (no grouping to fight the delimiter), dates as ISO, headers localized via the caller's `{{t}}`. `TestCSVEscapingRoundTrips` builds a cell holding `a,b"c\nd` (comma + quote + newline), writes, re-parses with `csv.Reader`, and asserts byte-identity — plus `-50.00` (signed) and a Blank money cell → empty string (distinct from a formatted zero). `reportCSV` streams it as `text/csv` with a `_smoke.csv` attachment filename.
  - **Shared params form — SCOPE always, the rest gated by ParamsSpec:** rendered on EVERY report (`report.tmpl`) as a plain `<form method="get">` (no JS, strict CSP — rule 12) submitting query params back to the same report. The **subsidiary SCOPE selector is UNCONDITIONAL** (`select[name=scope]`, D18 — every report is scoped) and is what `TestScopeSelectorOnEveryReport` asserts across `reports.Default().All()` (so a p15.3+ report is covered automatically). Defaults (`resolveParams`): scope = the user's `DefaultSubsidiaryID` else the root (`SubTree[0]`, pre-order); as-of = today; period = year-to-date; target currency = the scope subsidiary's `base_currency` (D18). Date inputs are plain text (never `input[type=date]` — rule 10/12), formatted per the user's setting. `ParamsSpec.{AsOf,Period,Granularity,Currency}` toggle the remaining controls.
  - **Toolkit = store + resolved params; p15.2 fills the methods.** `reports.NewToolkit(st, params)` holds the read-only store and the run's `Params`. p15.1 exposes `Store()` so the smoke report reads a REAL balance (`SubtreeBalancesAsOf` on the resolved scope) end-to-end; p15.2 GROWS the Toolkit with the Appendix-E methods (`BalancesAsOf/Activity/Rollup/NetIncome/FundBalances/FunctionalMatrix/ProgramActivity/Group990/IntercompanyNet`) over the p08.4 queries with D12 conversion + descendant-closure consolidation (D18) + D19 collapse, and real reports (p15.3+) call THOSE instead of `Store()` (kept a narrow accessor so the migration is a compile-time nudge).
  - **The ONE example report is a THROWAWAY placeholder (`_smoke`), NOT the trial balance.** `reports.SmokeReportID = "_smoke"` (leading underscore marks it internal/placeholder; title key explicitly labelled "placeholder") exercises typed cells (text + money + indent + subtotal), both renderers, the route, and the matrix — proving the framework end to end without pre-empting p15.3 (which OWNS the `trial-balance` id and shape). A later step deletes `smoke.go` + its `Default()` registration and the framework carries on unchanged.
  - **"Registry sync creates groups" is asserted at the DB layer** (`TestReportGroupsSynced`): after the startup `SyncReportGroups`, `store.ReportGroupNames` returns EXACTLY the four `reports.Groups()` in declared order — not just the one group the smoke report references — so `funds`/`programs`/`tax` land in `report_groups` before any report uses them (a grant FK is valid the moment p15.3+ or an admin references them).
  - **TDD deviation recorded (AGENTS DoD):** the `internal/reports` package tests were written alongside implementation and the first run was GREEN (the core types are pure data + small functions with no prior symbol to fail against), rather than observed-failing-first. The web-layer tests (`reports_test.go`) and the required listed tests (unknown-id-404, scope-selector-on-every-report, CSV escaping, group sync) DID drive behavior and are the real coverage; the deviation is the package-internal unit tests only.
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `encoding/csv` only); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged; no sqlc/query changes. New i18n keys `reports.*` in BOTH catalogs (`reports.params.*`, `reports.gran.*`, `reports.export.csv`, `reports.empty`, `reports.smoke.*` — group NAMES are raw reference values, not catalog entries; no dotted-key/leaf collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); the full parallel e2e suite (29 specs incl. the new `reports` spec — opens the smoke report, asserts the params form + scope selector + table, downloads the CSV) green 20×.

- **p15.2 (reports: toolkit)** — The Appendix-E computation core (`internal/reports/compute.go`) that all nine Phase-15 reports (p15.3–p15.11) call: consolidation (D18), conversion (D12), intercompany collapse (D19), effective-990 rollup (D25), placeholder tree rollups — in ONE place, so a report never re-derives them. Non-obvious calls:
  - **Method signatures (grown on `*Toolkit`, all pure reads, rule 2), dates as STRINGS:** `BalancesAsOf(ctx, Scope, asof, ConvertOpts) (map[AccountID][]CurAmt, error)`; `Activity(ctx, Scope, from, to, ConvertOpts) (map[AccountID][]CurAmt, error)`; `FundBalancesAsOf(ctx, Scope, asof, ConvertOpts) (map[FundID][]CurAmt, error)` (fund id 0 = unrestricted, D20); `FunctionalMatrix(ctx, Scope, from, to, ConvertOpts) (map[AccountID]map[Class][]CurAmt, error)`; `ProgramActivity(ctx, Scope, from, to, ConvertOpts) (map[ProgramID]map[AccountID][]CurAmt, error)`; `Group990(ctx, part, currency, map[AccountID]int64) ([]LineRow, error)`; `IntercompanyNet(ctx, Scope, asof) ([]CurAmt, error)`; `NetIncome(ctx, Scope, from, to, ConvertOpts) (CurAmt, error)`; `Rollup(ctx, currency, map[AccountID]int64) ([]TreeRow, error)`; `ByPeriod(from, to, Granularity, func(pFrom, pTo string) error) error`; `RateOn(ctx, base, quote, d) (Rate, error)`; plus `ConvertMinorAt(ctx, minor, from, to, d) (int64, error)` and exported `RoundHalfEven(float64) int64`. Types: `Scope{Sub SubsidiaryID}`, `ConvertOpts{To string; Mode RateMode(None|Closing|TxnDate)}`, `Class string`, `CurAmt{Currency string; Minor int64}`, `LineRow{Code; Amount CurAmt; Unmapped bool}`, `TreeRow{AccountID; Name; Amount CurAmt; Indent; Subtotal bool}`, `Rate{Rate; RateDate; Reciprocal}`.
  - **Appendix-E DEVIATION (recorded):** the sketch names `ledger.Date` and sketch return types (a bare `CurAmt`/`Rate`/`LineRow`); there is NO `ledger.Date` type — the p08.4 balance queries and `RateOn` already take **YYYY-MM-DD strings**, so the toolkit does too (matching the actual store API is the right call; Appendix E is explicitly a sketch). The value types (`CurAmt`, `Rate`, `LineRow`, `TreeRow`) are defined in the reports package. Balance/activity methods return a `[]CurAmt` per key (one entry per native currency; a converting mode collapses to a single target-currency entry). `Group990` takes an already-converted leaf map (single currency) so it does no conversion. Ids are plain `int64` aliases (`AccountID`/`FundID`/`ProgramID`/`SubsidiaryID`).
  - **Consolidation needs NO scope expansion here (D18):** the p08.4 queries ALREADY close the subsidiary descendant set with a recursive CTE (p08.4 note), so every method forwards `Scope.Sub` straight to the store. Root scope = full org; a leaf = just that sub. Proven by `TestBalancesAsOfRootVsLeafScope`: at ROOT every `Expected.AccountBalances` reproduces exactly; at the MX-leaf scope the MX-only accounts keep the SAME native balance (single-sub accounts are scope-invariant) while US-only accounts (CheckingUS/Building/DueFromMX/CreditCard) are ABSENT — the discriminating descendant-closure check.
  - **Conversion (D12) rounds HALF-EVEN at the FINAL AGGREGATE, via `money.ConvertMinor`** (the existing exponent-aware `math.RoundToEven` primitive — the ONLY float touch, rule 3). Grain: `Mode:Closing` converts EACH output cell (per fund/account per currency) once at the as-of on-or-before rate (`RateOn`), then sums the int64 results — the same grain the p14.1 seam blesses (`ConvertedFundBalances` are per-fund unrounded floats "p15 rounds"). `Mode:TxnDate` decomposes the period into calendar MONTHS via `ByPeriod(GranMonth)`, accumulates the UNROUNDED `Σ(monthNative·monthRate·10^(expTo−expFrom))` per output cell, and `RoundToEven`s ONCE — never per-month int64 rounding (that would round intermediately, violating "at final aggregates"). Under on-or-before lookup with the fixture's monthly rate schedule, month-granularity IS exactly per-transaction-date (every txn in month M resolves to the M-01 point). A missing rate surfaces `store.ErrRateMissing` (wrapped in-chain) so a report footnotes the gap, not a silent zero.
  - **Conversion oracles (hand-computed, fixture-derived):** `TestFundBalancesClosingConversion` — BecaAgua MXN 9,700,000 ÷ 18.10 = 535,911.60.. → **535,912**; unrestricted MXN 30,940,000 ÷ 18.10 = 1,709,392.26.. → **1,709,392**; USD legs pass through (asserted against `Expected.Rates.ConvertedFundBalances`). `TestActivityTxnDate` — Food Purchases MXN activity 120,000@2025-03 + 90,000@2025-04 + 150,000@2026-03 at rates 17.1294.../17.1941.../17.9059.. → unrounded 20,616.978.. → **20,617 USD**; PLUS a **grain-lock** on Cash MXN (whose monthly activity makes the two grains DIVERGE: per-month-rounded = 38,971, accumulate-then-round-ONCE = 38,970 — asserts **38,970**, discriminating the correct final-aggregate grain from per-month rounding; verified failing under a per-month-rounding mutation). `TestNetIncomeClosing` — native R/E subtotals USD −3,567,500 + MXN −9,140,000; MXN→USD ÷18.10 = −504,972.37.. → −504,972; total **−4,072,472 USD**. `TestRoundHalfEven` pins the tie-to-even + sign symmetry.
  - **Effective 990 code (D25):** `Group990` reuses the store's `Effective990Codes` walk (own code, else nearest ancestor's), rolls the leaf map by effective code (absent → `""` = the explicit **Unmapped** bucket), orders rows by `form990_lines(sort,code)` (via `codeOrder`, unioning the account-type-filtered line reads) with Unmapped ALWAYS last. `TestGroup990Effective` (Part IX): Salaries→IX.7, Occupancy→IX.16, **Bank Fees→IX.11g (LEAF OVERRIDE lands on its own line, NOT folded into the Expenses parent's IX.24e)**, Program Supplies+Insurance+Event Costs inherit IX.24e = 370,000. `TestGroup990Unmapped` (Part VIII): Event Income (the fixture's deliberately-unmapped R/E leaf, Z19) is the LAST row, code `""`, `Unmapped=true`, −300,000 — never dropped.
  - **Intercompany (D19):** `IntercompanyNet` reads the flagged account ids (new `IntercompanyAccountIDs` store method + ASCII positional query) and sums THEIR as-of balances per currency across the consolidated scope. `TestIntercompanyNetBalanced` → 0 USD on the clean fixture (Due-from +1,000,000 nets Due-to −1,000,000, `Expected.IntercompanyNetCurrencies`). `TestIntercompanyNetCorrupted` builds the nonzero case CORRECTLY: you can't post an unbalanced txn (zero-sum enforced) and net-to-zero is a CROSS-transaction property, so it posts ONE extra **balanced** txn (DR Due-from +250,000 / CR Checking US −250,000) with no mirroring Due-to credit — each txn stays zero-sum, but the consolidated intercompany net becomes +250,000 USD → the caller renders a `RowWarning`.
  - **Program rollup (D24):** `ProgramActivity` folds each program's raw cells UP the program tree (a parent includes descendants), so General (the seeded root) carries the whole org's program activity while leaf programs (Educación/Food Pantry) equal the raw `Expected.Program` oracle. `TestProgramActivity` asserts leaves against the oracle and General's hand-computed folded totals (e.g. Program Supplies USD 60,000 General-raw + 150,000 Educación = 210,000; Food Purchases MXN 210,000 + 150,000 = 360,000). `Rollup` walks the ACCOUNT tree pre-order emitting a `Subtotal` row per placeholder (subtree leaf sum) in tree order + leaf data rows; `TestRollupTreeOrder`: the Expenses placeholder subtotal = 2,327,500 (all expense leaves) and precedes its children.
  - **TDD (observed):** the tests carry hand-computed fixture-derived numbers; breaking the rounding primitive (`RoundToEven`→`Floor−1`) fails `TestRoundHalfEven`/`TestNetIncomeClosing`/`TestFundBalancesClosingConversion`/`TestActivityTxnDate`, confirming they are load-bearing (not tautological). No report pages/templates/goldens/e2e (those are p15.3+). Currency exponents cached per run (`Toolkit.expCache`). ISO date arithmetic (`ByPeriod` month decomposition) uses `time.Parse("2006-01-02")` — internal compute, not a user-render path (rule 10 governs display), the same pattern `store.transactions` validates dates with.
  - **One sqlc query added** (`IntercompanyAccountIDs`, ASCII, positional, `make gen` reproducible); no other query changes; no new dependencies; `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists).

- **p15.3 (report: trial balance) + the Phase-15 GOLDEN-FILE harness** — The FIRST real financial report (`internal/reports/trial_balance.go`), replacing the p15.1 `_smoke` placeholder, plus the golden convention p15.4–p15.11 copy. Non-obvious calls:
  - **`_smoke` is FULLY removed.** `internal/reports/smoke.go` deleted; `reports.Default()` now registers `registerTrialBalance` (id `reports.TrialBalanceReportID = "trial_balance"`, group `financial`, `ParamsSpec{AsOf, Currency}`) instead of the smoke report; the `reports.smoke.*` i18n keys are gone from BOTH catalogs (replaced by `reports.trial_balance.*`); `web/reports_test.go`'s three smoke tests are repointed to trial balance (a real balancing table over the seeded 2-account posting) with the `trial_balance.csv` download filename; `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` targets `/reports/trial_balance`. `routes_test.go`'s remaining `_smoke` mentions were COMMENTS ONLY (the matrix iterates real routes and the ReportsOnly persona's `financial` grant covers trial balance automatically — zero logic change); the `grp="placeholder"` in the decide-logic unit table is unrelated and untouched.
  - **Row model = one row per (account, currency); columns Account | Currency | Native | Converted.** A multi-currency account (FX Clearing holds USD 9,740 AND MXN 5,000) can't collapse into one money cell, so each (account, currency) is its own row. An EXPLICIT Currency text column is mandatory because the CSV writer emits money as a bare number with NO currency code (native "5000.00" vs a USD converted "276.24" would otherwise be ambiguous in the golden). Balances are **net-debit SIGNED** int64 minor units (D2: assets/expenses +, revenue/liability/equity −) in a single column — the task's "or signed per the net-debit convention"; no debit/credit split columns. Rows are emitted in ACCOUNT-TREE PRE-ORDER (walking `store.Tree(ctx, lang, nil)` and looking up each account's balances) so the output is DETERMINISTIC — `BalancesAsOf` returns a map, and Go map iteration is randomized, so relying on its order would flake the golden; currencies within an account are sorted.
  - **Converted column = per-cell `ConvertMinorAt`, a documented DEVIATION from the task's "use `BalancesAsOf(RateClosing)`".** `BalancesAsOf(RateClosing)` COLLAPSES a multi-currency account to ONE summed target-currency cell, which destroys the per-currency row alignment this report needs, so the report calls `tk.ConvertMinorAt(ctx, amt.Minor, amt.Currency, target, asof)` per (account, currency) cell instead. The arithmetic is IDENTICAL — `convertClosing` (what RateClosing uses) IS `ConvertMinorAt`-per-currency-then-sum — so this is a presentation choice, not a numeric one (D12 half-even at the final cell is preserved). Same toolkit, same rule.
  - **Lang plumbing: a new `Params.Lang` field (the pattern p15.4+ inherit).** This is the first report to render STORED per-language account names (`account_names`, resolved via `store.Tree(ctx, lang, …)`). `Run(ctx, tk, p)` has no `lang`, the lang ctx key is web-package-private, and AGENTS forbids smuggling anything but the actor through ctx — so `Params` grew a `Lang` field the web layer sets from `langOf(ctx)` in `resolveParams`, read via `p.LangOr()` (defaults "en" so a hand-built zero Params still resolves names). Every p15.4+ report that names accounts uses this.
  - **The trial balance BALANCES (asserted, the whole point):** the native per-currency SIGNED sum is exactly 0 (integer double-entry, D2). `TestTrialBalanceGolden` re-sums the report's OWN emitted native cells (`reports.SumMoneyColumn` over DATA rows — so a dropped/duplicated row is caught, not just the report's own total rows) and asserts **USD sum = 0 AND MXN sum = 0**, and that exactly those two currencies appear. The report emits a `RowSubtotal` "Total (native)" row per currency (each 0) plus a `RowTotal` "Total (converted)" grand total.
  - **HAND-VERIFIED converted figures (derived from the fixture natives + the 2026-06-30 closing USD→MXN rate 18.10, MXN→USD = 1/18.10, half-even at the cell — NOT read from code):** Checking MX 39,500,000 MXN → **2,182,320 USD**; Government Grants −10,000,000 MXN (its MXN leg) → **−552,486 USD**; Food Purchases 360,000 MXN → **19,890 USD**. The CONVERTED grand total is **0** on this fixture — the per-account MXN rounding residuals CANCEL — but that is a data property (asserted only after an in-test re-sum confirms it), NOT a guarantee: a future report whose residuals don't cancel would need a translation-adjustment line. A report is a trial balance because its NATIVE per-currency sums are zero; the converted total is presented so a reviewer sees the statement reconciled in one currency.
  - **GOLDEN HARNESS (the reusable Phase-15 deliverable, `internal/reports/golden.go` + `internal/reports/testdata/`):** two committed, human-REVIEWABLE artifacts per report — `<id>.txt` (an aligned fixed-width column dump via `reports.DumpTable`: the readable native+converted side-by-side view a reviewer scans, with `>`/`=`/`!` row-kind markers) and `<id>.csv` (the machine export via `reports.WriteCSV`). Both are DETERMINISTIC: the golden test PINS lang=en, as-of 2026-06-30, root scope, USD target, and formats money with a FIXED `reports.GoldenMoneyOpts` (NumberUS/Minus/Signed — NOT per-user settings, so no locale drift). Regeneration: a `-update` test flag rewrites the files; `make golden` runs `go test ./internal/reports/ -run Golden -update` (the Makefile stub is now implemented) — verified idempotent (a second `make golden` produces NO diff). The golden ENCODES CORRECTNESS: the key totals (native 0 per currency, converted 0, the three converted cells) are hand-derived from the fixture and asserted BEFORE the file comparison, so the golden isn't just a snapshot of whatever the code emits. DATA RULE 11: every value derives from the synthetic Appendix-D fixture (via `f.ExtendRates` for the rate column), so the goldens are safe to commit. p15.4–p15.11 copy this pattern (their own `testdata/<id>.{txt,csv}`, the same `checkGolden`/`DumpTable`/`-update`/`make golden` mechanism).
  - **Scope test reuses the toolkit consolidation:** `TestTrialBalanceScope` runs the report at ROOT vs the RV Mexico LEAF (native mode, rate-independent) and asserts the account SETS differ — MX-only accounts (Checking MX, Cash MXN, Due to RV Internacional) appear at both, US-only accounts (Checking US, Building, Due from RV Mexico, Credit Card) appear at root but are ABSENT from the MX leaf (descendant closure of MX excludes US, D18), and the leaf set is a strict subset. `TestTrialBalanceCSVParses` re-reads the report's CSV with `csv.Reader` and re-sums the native column to zero per currency — the balancing property survives the export.
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `encoding/csv`, `flag`, `os`, `path/filepath` only); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged; no sqlc/query changes. New i18n keys `reports.trial_balance.*` in BOTH catalogs (title/col.account/col.currency/col.native/col.converted/total_native/total_converted — `reports.trial_balance.title` is a leaf, never a bare `reports.trial_balance` prefix-and-leaf collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists). **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (repointed): an admin opens the trial balance, sets as-of/scope params, sees the params form + scope selector + table + a balancing total row, and the `.csv` endpoint returns `text/csv` — STRUCTURAL assertions (the fresh worker db has no seeded ledger, so specific numbers would be brittle), READ-ONLY (no worker-db leak). Full parallel suite green 15×.

- **p15.3d (reports: drill-down — framework capability)** — Every report balance/activity figure "clicks through" to the transactions that produce it: a filtered split list whose signed NATIVE sum EQUALS the figure. Built framework-FIRST so p15.4–p15.11 and the Phase-19 budget reports inherit it; only the trial balance is retrofitted here. Non-obvious calls:
  - **The `Drill` shape (`internal/reports/drill.go`) is pure, data-only, query-string-serializable.** `Drill{Scope int64, AccountIDs []int64, Currency string, FundID/ProgramID/Class *…, Mode DrillMode (DrillAsOf|DrillPeriod), AsOf/From/To string}`. It reconstructs ONE cell's figure: the scope (descendant closure D18), the account SET the cell sums (one id for a leaf cell; a subtree for a future rollup cell), the cell's NATIVE currency (REQUIRED for a money cell), and optional fund/program/class narrowing. `Mode` picks the date treatment (as-of cumulative vs period activity) so the drilled split set matches the toolkit method that produced the cell. `Encode()` → a stable-key query string; `DecodeDrill(url.Values)` is its FORGIVING inverse (a malformed id/date is dropped, so a tampered URL degrades to an empty list — a 200, not a 500 — and the permission matrix's BARE `/reports/{id}/drill` hit decodes to a zero drill = empty result). It carries NO store/HTTP, so the reconciliation invariant is unit-testable and the CSV/text renderers ignore it entirely (**golden UNCHANGED** — confirmed by `make golden` no-diff; drill links live only in the HTML `Cell.Drill` path).
  - **A `Cell` gains an optional `*Drill` + a `WithDrill(d)` builder.** `MoneyCell(m, ccy).WithDrill(&Drill{…})` opts a cell in; a nil `Drill` = not drillable (labels, totals). Keeping it a method (not a `MoneyCell` param) means the many non-drillable call sites are untouched and only drillable cells opt in — the p15.4+ attach pattern. The HTML renderer (`web/renderCell`, now threaded `reportID`) emits `renderedCell.Href = "/reports/"+id+"/drill?"+Drill.Encode()`; `report.tmpl` renders a drillable cell as a plain `<a class="report-drill-link" href=…>` (strict CSP — NO inline handler). CSV/`DumpTable` read only `Text`/`Minor` and never see `Drill`.
  - **PER-REPORT drill route + STATIC perm (not a dynamic-perm endpoint) — the rationale.** `routes.go` auto-mounts `GET /reports/{id}/drill` alongside the existing page + `.csv`, gated by the SAME `ReportGroup(report.Group)` as the report. So drill visibility EQUALS report visibility ("a viewer who can see the number can drill it"), and — being a CONCRETE registry route — it is permission-matrix-checked with ZERO test edits: `TestPermissionMatrix` hits `/reports/trial_balance/drill` bare (decodes to an empty drill → 200 empty list for an authorized persona, 403 for an ungranted one). A single dynamic `/reports/drill?…` endpoint was REJECTED — its Perm couldn't be static per report-group, so the matrix couldn't cover it. The drill handler needs its OWN path parse (`reportDrillFromPath`: strip `/reports/` prefix + `/drill` suffix); the existing `reportFromPath` strips `.csv` and would mis-parse `{id}/drill`.
  - **The store query (`DrillSplits`, `internal/db/queries/balances.sql` + `store/balances.go`) MIRRORS `SubtreeBalancesAsOf`/`PeriodActivity`, NOT `RegisterPage`.** The critical correctness point: the trial balance at ROOT scope sums an account over the subsidiary DESCENDANT CLOSURE (the recursive `scope` CTE), and one account can carry splits across several subs in that closure. `RegisterPage` filters ONE subsidiary by equality — reusing it would UNDER-count at root scope and break reconciliation. So `DrillSplits` uses the SAME recursive `scope(id)` CTE + `t.subsidiary_id IN (SELECT id FROM scope)`, `t.deleted = 0`, filtered to `sp.account_id = ?` AND **`t.currency = ?`** (each toolkit cell is per-currency — FX Clearing holds USD AND MXN, so only the currency-filtered sum equals a single cell), an as-of OR period date bound, and optional fund/program/class — returning the raw UNGROUPED splits ordered `(date, split_id)` (the store sums them). Optional filters use the paired-`?` active-flag trick (`(? = 0 OR col = ?)`) because sqlc's sqlite parser mangles a reused `?` (p04.2). A zero `AccountID` short-circuits to no rows (the empty/matrix hit). `balances.sql` stays pure ASCII (p04.2); `make gen` reproducible.
  - **Handler + render reuse the register row shape.** `web/reports_drill.go`: decode → `store.DrillFilter` → `DrillSplits` per account (bounded: one today) → `renderDrillRows` (mirrors `registerRows`' name-map + counter-account resolution: date/sub-badge/payee/memo/counter-or-"Split"/fund-chip/amount) → `report-drill.tmpl`, each row linking to the txn editor + history (p12.4). The header echoes the RECONCILED figure — the signed sum of the SAME rows shown — so header and list are provably consistent.
  - **RECONCILIATION invariant (the key test, `web/reports_drill_test.go` `TestDrillReconcilesToToolkit`):** for selected trial-balance cells over the fixture at ROOT scope, `Σ DrillSplits.Amount == tk.BalancesAsOf(RateNone)` native figure for that `(account, currency)` — the toolkit is the oracle, not the drill's own output. Covers a single-currency account (Checking MX 39,500,000 MXN), a MULTI-currency account (FX Clearing MXN 500,000 — reconciles ONLY because currency is filtered; an explicit check proves its MXN ≠ USD 974,000 drill), and a fund/program/class-narrowed PERIOD drill (proving the optional filters + the From/To date mode don't silently drop rows). HTTP tests assert the route lists rows with editor/history links, echoes the figure, and 200s on the bare hit.
  - **CONVERTED/CONSOLIDATED cells drill to NATIVE splits (framework rule; retrofit drills the native cell only).** The reconciliation invariant is against the PRE-conversion native figure — a cell the report showed converted (D12) still lists the native underlying transactions; the drill header carries a `Converted` annotation (i18n `reports.drill.native_note`) for a later report that drills a converted column. The trial-balance retrofit attaches `Drill` to the NATIVE money cell only (the converted column is left non-drillable — the native drill already covers the transactions); `nativeDrill = &Drill{Scope: p.Scope, AccountIDs: []int64{node.ID}, Currency: a.Currency, Mode: DrillAsOf, AsOf: p.AsOf}`. **p15.4–p15.11 attach `Drill` the same way** — a `MoneyCell(…).WithDrill(&Drill{…})` on their balance/activity cells, `DrillPeriod` (From/To) for activity reports, `FundID`/`ProgramID`/`Class` set for narrowed cells.
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `net/url`, `sort`, `strconv`, `strings`); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. New i18n keys `reports.drill.{title,figure,native_note,empty}` in BOTH catalogs (all leaves under `reports.drill.*`, no dotted-key/leaf collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): seeds a balanced transfer (two unique-named accounts + one txn), opens the trial balance at the default as-of, clicks a `.report-drill-link`, lands on the drill list, and sees rows each linking to the editor/history — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), mutating but only ADDING uniquely-named rows (inert to sibling reads). Full parallel suite green **15×** (450/450).

- **p15.4 (report: balance sheet)** — The statement of financial position (`internal/reports/balance_sheet.go`), the second real financial statement, copying the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns. Non-obvious calls:
  - **Net-asset classification is BY RESTRICTION, and the identity is STRUCTURAL, not lucky (the accounting trap).** Sections are ASSETS, LIABILITIES, NET ASSETS. Assets/Liabilities list their account rows (net-debit signs, D2: assets stored positive; a liability's stored credit is NEGATED to read as a positive balance). NET ASSETS is the nonprofit split (Q3, D20): **Net assets with donor restrictions** = Σ the RESTRICTED funds' asset-side (unexpended) `FundBalancesAsOf` balances (a fund is restricted when its `Restriction` field is non-empty — purpose/time/perpetual; fund id 0 excluded), via a new `Toolkit.restrictedNetAssets`. **Total net assets** = the PLUG `(Assets − Liabilities)` taken from the already-collapsed section totals — NOT a fund-balance sum. **Net assets without donor restrictions** = total − with. This is deliberate: `FundBalancesAsOf` is ASSET-side only (a whole-fund sum is zero by conservation), so it sums to total ASSETS, not net assets — a naive "without = fund 0" is off by exactly the liabilities. **The discriminator (asserted in `TestBalanceSheetNativeSplit`):** on the fixture USD, without = 17,217,500 while fund-0 = 18,517,500 (differ by the 1,300,000 of USD liabilities); on MXN they accidentally coincide (30,940,000) because MXN liabilities are zero — so a "without = fund 0" bug passes MXN and fails USD, and the test asserts USD without ≠ 18,517,500 explicitly. Because NA is the plug of the collapsed sections, the identity `Assets = Liabilities + (without + with)` holds by construction and stays consistent through intercompany collapse and FX conversion.
  - **Equity-source accounts are NOT emitted as rows.** Only `asset`/`liability`-type accounts get rows; `equity`/`revenue`/`expense` accounts (Opening Balances, the R/E leaves) are ABSORBED into the net-asset plug. Emitting Opening Balances (−18,700,000 USD equity) alongside the synthetic by-restriction lines would double-count and break the identity (net assets decompose two ways — by restriction {without+with} and by source {opening+surplus} — both summing to 22,267,500; the E section shows the BY-RESTRICTION split only). A test asserts no `Opening Balances` row appears.
  - **"Net surplus to date" is a DISCLOSURE, not a peer of the totals.** It is `NetIncome`-from-inception (cumulative R/E activity to the as-of date, presented POSITIVE since a surplus is a net credit), rendered as an indented "of which" memo under without-restriction and NOT summed into any total (a new `Toolkit.netSurplusByCurrency`; `inceptionDate = "1900-01-01"` as the lower bound — on-or-before every possible txn, so it is truly cumulative-from-inception without per-org config). Hand-verified on the fixture: 3,567,500 USD / 9,140,000 MXN.
  - **Intercompany collapse + warning (D19), gated on CONSOLIDATED (multi-sub) scope.** D19 says "collapse flagged accounts", so at a consolidated scope the intercompany-flagged due-to/due-from accounts are ELIMINATED — dropped from the Assets/Liabilities LISTINGS and their section totals (not shown as rows), via `store.IntercompanyAccountIDs` skipped in the classification walk. On the balanced fixture they net to zero, so total net assets is unchanged and only the Assets/Liabilities totals shrink by the eliminated 1,000,000 USD each (root golden: Total assets 248,128.04, Total liabilities 3,000.00, NA 245,128.04 — identity holds). The residual (`Toolkit.IntercompanyNet`, computed only at a consolidated scope) is surfaced as a `RowWarning` (`role="alert"`, never hidden) when NONZERO. **Scope gate (a bug fixed on advisor review):** "consolidated" = the scope's descendant closure has >1 subsidiary (`Toolkit.isConsolidated` via `store.Descendants`). At a LEAF/single-sub scope the intercompany accounts are that sub's GENUINE due-to-parent / due-from-child balances — SHOWN as ordinary rows, NOT collapsed, and NEVER warned (an earlier version warned at leaf scope because `IntercompanyNet(leaf)` sees only one side, −1,000,000 ≠ 0 — a false positive; `TestBalanceSheetScope` now pins `warningRow(leafTable) == nil` AND that Due-to is shown at the leaf but collapsed at root). Warning tested clean-vs-corrupted (`TestBalanceSheetIntercompanyWarning`) via p15.2's corrupted-copy technique: post ONE extra BALANCED txn (DR Due-from +250,000 / CR Checking US −250,000) with no mirroring Due-to credit — each txn stays zero-sum but the consolidated intercompany net becomes +250,000 USD → the warning row appears carrying the 250,000 residual. Absent on the clean fixture.
  - **Per-currency DETAIL toggle = a new framework param.** `Run` only sees `Params`, so the toggle is a new `Params.Detail` string (`""` = converted-only, `"currency"` = per-currency) gated by a new `ParamsSpec.Detail`, parsed in `web/resolveParams`, surfaced as a `<select name="detail" class="report-detail-select">` in `report.tmpl` (mirroring the Currency/Granularity wiring). Converted-only mode = 2 columns `[Line, Amount(converted at AsOf closing rate, D12)]`; detail mode = 4 columns `[Line, Currency, Native, Converted]` expanding each line per native currency (the first currency row carries the label, continuations blank-named). The **net-asset total is the plug of the NATIVE sections, then converted per-currency once at the closing rate** (each currency converted once, then summed) — NOT per-line residual cancellation. The converted identity `Assets = Liabilities + NetAssets` holds on this fixture (asserted by the hardcoded converted `wantConv`), which is why the golden pins the converted totals directly rather than relying on `round(A−L) == round(A)−round(L)` in general. Recorded as a framework touch (a fourth optional shared param alongside AsOf/Period/Granularity/Currency).
  - **Drill (p15.3d) on asset/liability ACCOUNT cells only.** Each account cell carries a `Drill{Scope, AccountIDs:[id], Currency, Mode:DrillAsOf, AsOf}` (the trial-balance retrofit shape) reconciling to the account's native figure; in converted-only mode a single-currency account drills its one currency, a multi-currency account (FX Clearing) is left non-drillable there (one link can't reconcile a summed-across-currencies converted figure — the detail view is its drill path). The synthetic net-asset lines are NOT drillable (they span many funds/accounts, no single `DrillFilter`). Reconciliation proven in `web/reports_drill_test.go` `TestBalanceSheetDrillReconciles`: it runs the REAL report, pulls every drillable cell's `Drill`, and asserts `Σ store.DrillSplits == tk.BalancesAsOf` native for each (account, currency) — the toolkit is the oracle, not the report's output.
  - **Golden = converted-totals mode at root scope (the multicurrency, multi-sub case).** `internal/reports/testdata/balance_sheet.{txt,csv}` at lang=en, as-of 2026-06-30, root (US+MX / USD+MXN consolidation), USD target. Key totals hand-derived from the fixture natives + the 18.10 closing rate BEFORE the file comparison, POST intercompany elimination (converted USD minor: Assets 24,812,804; Liabilities 300,000; NA 24,512,804; without 18,926,892; with 5,585,912; surplus 4,072,472; L+NA = Assets). The detail mode is covered by `TestBalanceSheetDetailToggle` + `TestBalanceSheetNativeSplit` (native per-currency figures asserted directly against the oracle) rather than a second golden. A leaf-sub (RV Mexico) vs root scope difference is `TestBalanceSheetScope`.
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `context`, `sort`); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. New i18n keys `reports.balance_sheet.*` (title, `col.{line,amount,currency,native,converted}`, `section.{assets,liabilities,net_assets}`, `total.{assets,liabilities,net_assets,liabilities_net_assets}`, `na.{without,with,surplus_of_which}`, `intercompany_warning`) + `reports.params.detail` + `reports.detail.{converted,currency}` in BOTH catalogs (all leaves, no dotted-key/leaf collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): opens the balance sheet, asserts the three section labels + the with/without net-asset split labels + a balancing grand-total row, toggles `detail=currency` (asserts ≥4 columns + the select value), and fetches the CSV — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), READ-ONLY (mutates nothing durable). Full parallel suite green **15×** (6 full-suite runs of 31 tests + 9 targeted `reports` runs of 3 tests, all passed, no flakes).

- **p15.5 (report: income statement / statement of activities)** — The period P&L (`internal/reports/income_statement.go`), the third real financial statement, copying the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns. Non-obvious calls:
  - **TXN-DATE conversion for a FLOW (D12), NOT closing.** The balance sheet (a position) converts at the AsOf CLOSING rate; the income statement is a FLOW — each revenue/expense figure is converted at the rate on each transaction's DATE (`Toolkit.Activity(scope, from, to, ConvertOpts{To, Mode: RateTxnDate})`, the p15.2 month-decomposition), because income earned across a period is measured at the rate in force when it occurred. The hand-verified discriminator (`TestIncomeStatementGolden`): Food Purchases (MXN) whole-range activity converts to **20,616 USD** at txn-date but **19,890 USD** at closing — the test asserts the total column reproduces 20,616 and is NOT 19,890, proving the mode.
  - **COMPARATIVE COLUMNS via `ByPeriod`; the TOTAL column is Σ(period columns), NOT a fresh whole-range Activity call (the FOOTING rule — advisor-flagged).** With month/quarter granularity the period splits into calendar sub-periods (`Toolkit.ByPeriod`, the deterministic bucketing), one COLUMN each, each column = that sub-period's `Activity`. Under `RateTxnDate` the per-account converted figure is rounded half-even ONCE per `Activity` call (`compute.go`), so `round(Σ months)` ≠ `Σ round(month)`: building the Total column by ADDING the per-period converted cells (int64, no rounding) makes "**Σ period columns == total column, per row**" hold EXACTLY (`TestIncomeStatementComparativeColumns`). A statement that does not foot is wrong, so footing WINS over bit-equality with a whole-range `NetIncome`. Concretely the report NET (sum-of-quarters) = **4,099,507** differs by ONE minor unit from whole-range `NetIncome`-txn-date (4,099,506); the report's figure is authoritative. The EXACT, rate-independent cross-check is the NATIVE R/E net: USD 3,567,500 / MXN 9,140,000 (net-debit, presented positive), asserted directly against the fixture oracle (`TestIncomeStatementNativeNet`).
  - **MIXED R/E TREE PRESERVED (not flattened).** `runIncomeStatement` walks the account tree per section (`section(tree, "revenue"|"expense", …)`): the Revenue and Expenses PLACEHOLDER parents are `RowSubtotal` rows carrying their subtree's per-column sums, their children are indented `RowData` rows. A leaf is in-section only when it is of the section type AND carries activity in the scope (present in the converted-total map) — so a global chart-of-accounts leaf with no in-scope activity drops out (drives `TestIncomeStatementScope`: US-posted Contributions appears at root, absent at the RV-Mexico leaf). **Sign per section:** revenue activity is net-debit NEGATIVE (a credit) → display sign −1 (positive inflow); expense is net-debit POSITIVE (a debit) → sign +1; net surplus = −(revRaw + expRaw) = Revenue − Expense, positive = surplus, per column (`RowTotal`).
  - **Period COLUMN HEADERS are stable period IDENTIFIERS, not formatted dates.** A comparative column's header is `YYYY-Qn` (quarter) / `YYYY-MM` (month) — a period NAME (a coarse column marker), deterministic across locales, so it sidesteps rule 10 (which governs date/number RENDERING, not period identifiers) and needs no framework change to the header path (`Column.HeaderKey` surfaces an unknown key verbatim via `i18n.T`'s fallback). GranNone → a single "Period" column. The Total/section/net labels are real i18n keys.
  - **Drill (p15.3d) on single-native-currency R/E leaf cells, `DrillPeriod`.** Each drillable leaf cell carries `Drill{Scope, AccountIDs:[id], Currency, Mode:DrillPeriod, From, To}` — From/To = that column's sub-period range (or the whole [From,To] for the Total cell). Multi-currency leaves and all subtotal/net rows are non-drillable (one link can't reconcile a summed-across-currencies or rolled-up figure — the balance-sheet rule). Reconciliation proven in `web/reports_drill_test.go` `TestIncomeStatementDrillReconciles`: it runs the REAL report, pulls every drillable cell's `Drill`, and asserts `Σ store.DrillSplits == tk.Activity` NATIVE for each (account, currency) over that sub-period range (the report figure was CONVERTED but the drill lists NATIVE splits; the invariant holds against the pre-conversion native figure). Anchor: Food Purchases MXN whole-range drill = 360,000.
  - **Golden = quarterly comparative columns at root scope (`internal/reports/testdata/income_statement.{txt,csv}`)** at lang=en, period 2025-01-01..2026-06-30, USD target, txn-date. Six quarterly columns + Line + Total = 8 columns; key totals hand-derived from the fixture natives + the p14.1 monthly rate schedule BEFORE the file comparison (converted USD minor: Total revenue 6,476,594; Total expenses 2,377,087; Net 4,099,507; and the per-leaf totals). A leaf-sub vs root difference is `TestIncomeStatementScope`.
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `context`, `fmt`; `cuento/internal/store` for the tree-row shape — the same import `compute.go` already uses); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. The web layer needed ZERO changes — the shared params form already renders Granularity/Currency/Period generically from `ParamsSpec` (p15.1). New i18n keys `reports.income_statement.*` (title, `col.{line,period,total}`, `section.{revenue,expenses}`, `total.{revenue,expenses}`, `net`) in BOTH catalogs (all leaves, no dotted-key/leaf collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): opens the income statement at a fixed period + `granularity=quarter`, asserts the Revenue/Expenses/Net labels (the R/E tree), the comparative-column header count, a net (report-total) row, the granularity/from/to controls, and fetches the CSV — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), READ-ONLY. Full parallel suite green **15×** (32 tests/run, all passed, no flakes).

- **p15.6 (report: account ledger)** — A printable REGISTER for ONE account over a period (`internal/reports/account_ledger.go`), with opening/closing balances framing the in-range lines and a FUND column, copying the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns. Non-obvious calls:
  - **Account param = a report-SPECIFIC control, added to the framework as `ParamsSpec.Account` / `Params.Account`.** Unlike the always-present subsidiary scope, the ledger needs to name ONE account. `ParamsSpec` grew an `Account bool` gate and `Params` an `Account int64`; the web `resolveParams` parses `?account=` and VALIDATES it against the real LEAF-account set (`accountLedgerOptions` = accounts with no children, since splits post only to leaves — mirrors the reports `Rollup`/`indexTree` leaf derivation), dropping an arbitrary/non-leaf id. `report.tmpl` renders the account `<select class="report-account-select" name="account">` gated by `ShowAccount`, with a leading "Choose an account…" option (value 0). **No account chosen (Account == 0) ⇒ empty Table** (the framework's nothing-to-show rule), so the bare `/reports/account_ledger` hit renders 200 with just the form — `TestScopeSelectorOnEveryReport` and the permission matrix pass unchanged.
  - **Line → txn-editor link: a new `Cell.TxnID` + `WithTxn(id)` builder — a DISTINCT mechanism from `Drill`.** `Drill` links a cell to `/reports/{id}/drill` (the split list behind an AGGREGATE); a ledger LINE names ONE transaction the reviewer opens, so `DateCell(ln.Date).WithTxn(ln.TxnID)` carries the txn id and the web `renderCell` builds `/transactions/{TxnID}/edit` (p12.4) — URL construction stays in `web`, parallel to how `Drill.Encode()` is web-built (reports never names a route). A cell carries at most one of `Drill`/`TxnID`; CSV/`DumpTable` ignore both (golden unchanged). Opening/closing balance cells DO carry a `Drill{Mode: DrillAsOf, AsOf: dayBefore(from) | to}` (the pre-range / cumulative history behind the framing figures — the trial-balance retrofit shape). **Drill RECONCILIATION tested** (`TestAccountLedgerDrillReconciles`, the p15.3d invariant p15.4/p15.5 also carry): each framing cell's `Drill` is turned into a `store.DrillSplits` filter (as the web handler does), the contributing splits summed, and asserted `== cell.Minor` — the store query is the oracle, so a subtly-wrong opening/closing drill filter fails here (not just the descriptor-shape check). Anchors: opening drill → 40,000,000, closing drill → 39,500,000.
  - **Lines from `store.DrillSplits` (period mode), NOT `RegisterPage` — because of D18.** `DrillSplits` closes the scope's descendant set via a recursive CTE (respects D18 for a non-root scope); `RegisterPage`'s `Subsidiary` filter is EXACT-match (cannot express "sub + descendants") and restarts its running balance within the filtered range — both wrong for a scoped ledger. So lines = `DrillSplits{Scope, AccountID, Currency, From, To}` (it REQUIRES a currency filter — no active-flag on `Currency` — hence the per-currency loop), and opening/closing = `tk.BalancesAsOf(scope, dayBefore(from) | to, RateNone)`. The running balance is accumulated in Go (`running = opening; running += line.amount`), losing nothing vs RegisterPage's window function.
  - **The ledger IDENTITY = the correctness cross-check: `opening + Σ(range lines) == closing`, per currency, from TWO INDEPENDENT queries.** `cumulative(to) = cumulative(from−1) + activity(from..to)`, so the closing figure (a `BalancesAsOf` query) must equal opening (another `BalancesAsOf`) plus the sum of the DrillSplits line amounts — a real cross-check, not a tautology. `dayBefore(iso)` = `time.Parse("2006-01-02")` + `AddDate(0,0,-1)` (compute.go's internal ISO-string convention, not a user-render path). HAND-VERIFIED golden — **Checking MX** (single-currency MXN, MULTI-FUND) over a MID-FIXTURE range `from=2025-05-01, to=2026-06-30`: opening (as of 2025-04-30) = 30,000,000 (2025-01-01 open) + 10,000,000 (2025-04-01 Beca Agua grant) = **40,000,000**; the one in-range txn (2025-05-10 mixed-funding supplies) posts two Checking-MX legs −300,000 (fund **Beca Agua**, running 39,700,000) and −200,000 (**Unrestricted**, running 39,500,000); closing (as of 2026-06-30) = **39,500,000** == `Expected.AccountBalances{CheckingMX,MXN}` (the fixture oracle) == 40,000,000 + (−500,000). The chosen range STARTS MID-FIXTURE so opening is nonzero and only in-range lines list (a range-boundary test confirms `from=2025-01-01` instead yields opening 0 and 4 lines, closing unchanged).
  - **FUND column + MULTI-CURRENCY.** Each line's fund cell is `TextCell(fundName)` for a restricted split or `LabelCell("reports.account_ledger.unrestricted")` for a nil-fund split (the unrestricted group D20 is a synthetic LABEL, not a stored name — so it localizes). An account holding >1 currency (FX Clearing: USD + MXN) renders one SECTION per currency (`unionCurrencies(opening, closing)`, sorted), each with its OWN opening/lines/closing and an INDEPENDENT running balance — currencies never mix in one total (`TestAccountLedgerMultiCurrency` pins FX Clearing USD 974,000 and MXN 500,000 in two sections and asserts every line's amount/running cells share a currency). The report converts NOTHING (native amounts only — nothing in the step asks for conversion), so `ParamsSpec` sets `{Period, Account}`, no `Currency`.
  - **No new dependencies** (stdlib `context`, `sort`, `time`; `cuento/internal/store` for the `DrillRow`/`DrillFilter` shapes); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. New i18n keys `reports.account_ledger.*` (title, `col.{date,description,fund,amount,balance}`, `opening`, `closing`, `unrestricted`) + `reports.params.account` + `reports.account.choose` in BOTH catalogs (all leaves — `account` and `account_ledger` are distinct keys, no dotted-key/leaf collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): seeds two leaf accounts + a balanced transfer, opens the account ledger, picks the account via the selector + a period, asserts the opening (report-subtotal) / closing (report-total) framing rows, an in-range data line with the Unrestricted fund label + a `/transactions/{id}/edit` line link + a drill link, and fetches the CSV — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), MUTATES only unique-named rows (worker-db safe). Full parallel suite green **15×** (33 tests/run, all passed, no flakes).

- **p15.7 (report: functional expenses — IRS Form 990 Part IX)** — The Statement of Functional Expenses matrix (`internal/reports/functional_expenses.go`), the first report in the **`tax`** group, copying the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns. Non-obvious calls:
  - **ROW grouping = effective Part IX 990 line (D25), Unmapped bucket LAST; COLUMNS = the three functional classes + Total.** Expense accounts are bucketed by their EFFECTIVE Part IX code (own code, else nearest-ancestor's — a leaf override lands on its OWN line) via a new pass-through `Toolkit.EffectiveCodes` (wraps `store.Effective990Codes`); each present line renders a grouping/subtotal row (the IRS-seeded `<line> — <label>`) with its contributing accounts INDENTED beneath it, in the part's report order (`Toolkit.Part990Lines(ctx, "IX", "expense")`, sort from `form990_lines`), the `""` bucket appended LAST. Columns are `Program | Management & general | Fundraising | Total`; each cell = that (account/line)×(class) expense. The **class column headers REUSE the existing `functional.{program,management,fundraising}` catalog labels** (the same labels the txn editor shows) — no new class keys.
  - **CONVERSION = CLOSING rate to the target (default scope base), like the BALANCE SHEET, NOT the income statement's txn-date.** A 990 is single-currency and a Part IX line total is a year-end ROLLUP (a position-style aggregate), so `FunctionalMatrix(scope, from, to, {To: target, Mode: RateClosing})` converts each (account,class) cell once at the period-end closing rate (D12 final-aggregate grain). The **line subtotals, the Total column, and the grand total are built by INT64 ADDITION of the converted cells** (the income-statement "footing" rule), so `Program + Management + Fundraising == Total` holds EXACTLY per row and `Σ lines == grand total` exactly — no second rounding. `ParamsSpec = {Period, Currency}`.
  - **DRILL = account×class cell → `DrillPeriod{account, class, period, native ccy}` (reuses `DrillSplits`' class filter).** Only a SINGLE-native-currency cell drills (a cell mixing USD+MXN, e.g. Program Supplies×program, and the subtotal/grand rows are non-drillable — one currency-filtered link cannot reconcile a summed-across-currencies or rolled-up figure, the balance-sheet rule). `TestFunctionalExpensesDrillReconciles` turns the Salaries×program cell's `Drill` into a `store.DrillFilter{…, Class: &"program"}`, sums the contributing splits, and asserts `== cell.Minor` (== native 1,650,000, since USD is 1:1) — the store is the oracle.
  - **HAND-VERIFIED golden** (`testdata/functional_expenses.{txt,csv}`, root scope, period 2025-01-01..2026-06-30, USD target, closing rate 18.10 ⇒ MXN→USD = 1/18.10 half-even per (account,class) cell): **IX.7** Salaries program 1,650,000; **IX.11g** Bank Fees management 2,500 (the LEAF-OVERRIDE landing on its own line, D25 — its siblings inherit IX.24e); **IX.16** Occupancy management 305,000; **IX.24e** program 257,514 (= Program Supplies 210,000 USD + 500,000 MXN/18.10 = 27,624, + Food Purchases 360,000 MXN/18.10 = 19,890), management 60,000 (Insurance), fundraising 100,000 (Event Costs), line total 417,514. **GRAND** program 1,907,514 · management 367,500 · fundraising 100,000 · **total 2,375,014**. All hand-derived from `Expected.Functional` + the `Rollup990` Part IX lines + the p14.1 rate seam BEFORE the file comparison. **Unmapped bucket is EMPTY on this fixture** (every expense leaf inherits IX.24e from the Expenses parent — the single unmapped R/E leaf, Event Income, is REVENUE = Part VIII, not Part IX); `TestFunctionalExpensesUnmappedLast` proves the ordering MECHANISM directly against `Toolkit.Group990` (an absent-code account buckets to `""` and sorts LAST), and `TestFunctionalExpensesOrdering` asserts the real IX.7 < IX.11g < IX.16 < IX.24e order + the grand-total row is last.
  - **990-line labels = STORED reference data (TEXT), not catalog keys.** The `form990_lines.label` is IRS-seeded reference text (like a currency name or an account name — rule 9's stored-data carve-out), rendered verbatim as a `TextCell`; only the framework labels are catalog keys. This SIDESTEPS the dotted-key/leaf collision the codes would cause: a key like `IX.11g` parses as nested TOML tables (`IX` → `11g`), breaking the message-table structure — so codes are NEVER catalog keys. The web layer needed ZERO changes (the report auto-mounts under `tax`; the shared params form renders Period+Currency from `ParamsSpec`; the permission matrix picks up the new route). New i18n keys `reports.functional_expenses.{title,col.line,col.total,unmapped,total}` in BOTH catalogs (all leaves, no collision). No new dependencies (stdlib `context`, `sort`); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): creates an expense account with an effective Part IX line (IX.16 Occupancy) + a functional class, posts an expense txn, opens the report, asserts the `Line/Program/Management & general/Fundraising/Total` headers + the Occupancy 990-line row + the `Total functional expenses` grand row (report-total) + a 990-line report-subtotal row, and fetches the CSV — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), MUTATES only unique-named rows (worker-db safe). Full parallel suite green **15×** (6 report specs × 15 = 90 passed, no flakes).

- **p15.8 (report: fund balances & activity)** — The donor-restricted fund tracking / per-grant funder view (`internal/reports/fund_activity.go`), the first (only) report in the **`funds`** group, copying the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns and the p15.6 account-ledger's report-specific-selector shape. Non-obvious calls:
  - **TWO views selected by a new report-specific FUND param (`ParamsSpec.Fund`/`Params.Fund`, mirroring `Account`).** With NO fund chosen (`Fund == 0`) the report is the **LIST** (fund ROSTER): every fund's as-of (To) balance per currency + funder / restriction-kind / purpose metadata columns + the **Unrestricted line (fund 0)**, via `Toolkit.FundBalancesAsOf` + a new `fundMetaMap` (name/funder/restriction/purpose from `ListFunds`). Restriction-kind labels REUSE the existing `funds.restriction.{purpose,time,perpetual}` catalog labels (the funds-workspace ones) — no new restriction keys. With a fund chosen via `?fund=` the report is that fund's period **STATEMENT**. Web plumbing mirrors the account param exactly: `resolveParams` parses/validates `?fund=` against the real fund set (`fundActivityOptions`/`fundExists`, active+closed), the shared form renders a `<select name="fund">` with an "— all funds —" default (fund 0 is never a valid single selection), and `paramsForm` gains `ShowFund`/`Fund`/`Funds`.
  - **The single-fund STATEMENT tracks the fund's SPENDABLE (cash) position and derives the "applied" split from account TYPE (`Toolkit.FundPeriodStatement`).** It reads the fund's splits to To (`FundLedger`) + the account tree for types, classifies each in-period split, and folds: **Received** = −Σ(revenue splits) [+ liability draws] (a positive display of the net-debit credit); **Applied — expense** = Σ(expense splits, positive net-debit); **Applied — non-expense** = Σ(positive-net-debit DEBITS to a NON-CASH asset (or a liability principal paydown)) — a "capital" asset the fund receives a debit for on a DISBURSEMENT txn (no revenue split). **Opening/Closing (spendable)** = the fund's asset accounts EXCLUDING those capital targets. The **identity `Opening + Received − AppliedExpense − AppliedNonExpense == Closing` holds per currency BY CONSTRUCTION** (the fund nets to zero within itself, D20/Z10), asserted from the report's OWN emitted rows (three independent flow queries).
  - **The Building purchase lands in NON-EXPENSE, not expenses — the D20 "applied" derivation p15.9 consumes.** The fixture's Building Fund receipt (Checking +50,000 / Contributions −50,000, both fund-tagged) → Building asset purchase (Building +40,000 / Checking −40,000, both fund-tagged, no program) is an ASSET↔ASSET move that does NOT change the fund's ALL-asset balance, so a naive "applied = Δall-asset" would show the Building purchase as ZERO. The spendable model shows it as a **40,000 non-expense application** (a debit to the capital Building account on a disbursement), leaving spendable Closing 10,000. A **`Total fund assets` reconciliation row** (the all-asset `FundBalancesAsOf(To)` the LIST shows) proves **Closing (spendable) + Capitalized == all-asset balance** (10,000 + 40,000 == 50,000). For a CASH-ONLY fund (Beca Agua) spendable == all-asset, so its Closing EQUALS the as-of fund balance the roster shows (the literal "Closing == as-of fund balance" assertion holds where there is no capitalization).
  - **HAND-VERIFIED numbers** (root scope, native currency, period 2025-01-01..2026-06-30). **LIST golden** (`testdata/fund_activity.{txt,csv}`): Beca Agua MXN 97,000.00 (9,700,000) + USD 500.00 (50,000); Building Fund USD 50,000.00 (5,000,000); Unrestricted MXN 309,400.00 (30,940,000) + USD 185,175.00 (18,517,500) — every figure == `Expected.FundBalances`. **STATEMENT golden** (`testdata/fund_activity_statement.{txt,csv}`, Building Fund): Opening 0, Received 50,000.00, Applied-expense 0, **Applied-non-expense 40,000.00 (the Building purchase)**, Closing (spendable) 10,000.00, Total fund assets 50,000.00 — identity `0 + 50,000 − 0 − 40,000 == 10,000` ✓; reconcile `10,000 + 40,000 == 50,000` ✓ == `Expected.FundBalances{BuildingFund,USD}`. Beca Agua statement: MXN Received 100,000.00 − expense 3,000.00 == Closing 97,000.00; USD Received 2,000.00 − expense 1,500.00 == Closing 500.00 (== fixture oracle, cash-only).
  - **DRILL wiring.** LIST balance cells drill (`DrillAsOf{all-asset ids, fund, To}`) for RESTRICTED funds; the Unrestricted line (fund 0, NULL `fund_id`) is intentionally NON-drillable — `DrillSplits`' fund filter is `(? = 0 OR sp.fund_id = ?)` (0 = "no filter"), with NO NULL-fund predicate, so `fundIDForDrill(0)` returns nil and the cell stays plain rather than summing every fund. STATEMENT cells drill: Opening/Closing → `DrillAsOf{spendable ids, fund}`; Total-assets → `DrillAsOf{all-asset ids, fund}`; Applied-expense → `DrillPeriod{expense ids, fund}`; Applied-non-expense → `DrillPeriod{capital ids, fund}` (exactly the Building split, 4,000,000); Received → `DrillPeriod{revenue ids, fund}` (the received figure is a sign-flip of the raw revenue net-debit, so the drilled RAW splits sum to −5,000,000, the income-statement convention — the drill reconciles to the pre-display native figure). `TestFundActivityListDrillReconciles` + `TestFundStatementDrillReconciles` build each cell's `Drill` into a `store.DrillFilter` and assert the split sum == the cell (store is the oracle).
  - No new dependencies (stdlib `context`, `sort`), no new sqlc query (reuses `FundBalancesAsOf`/`FundLedger`/`DrillSplits`/`ListFunds`/`Tree`); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. New i18n keys `reports.params.fund` + `reports.fund_activity.{title,col.*,unrestricted,opening,received,applied_expense,applied_nonexpense,closing,total_assets,all_funds}` in BOTH catalogs (all leaves, no dotted-key collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): seeds a restricted fund + a receipt into it + a capital-asset PURCHASE from it, opens the LIST (fund selector + roster row + funder metadata + Unrestricted line), picks the fund → the STATEMENT with the applied SPLIT (Opening/Received/`Applied — expenses`/`Applied — non-expense`/Closing/Total fund assets labels + framing rows + a drill link), and fetches the CSV — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), MUTATES only unique-named rows (worker-db safe). Full parallel suite green **15×** (7 report specs × 15 = 105 passed, no flakes).

- **p15.9 (report: activities by restriction — FASB Statement of Activities)** — The net-asset flow statement (`internal/reports/activities_by_restriction.go`) with the two donor-restriction columns + a Total column, copying the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns. Non-obvious calls:
  - **GROUP = `financial`** (not `funds`). It is a core financial statement a 990 preparer reads alongside the trial balance / balance sheet / income statement; the code-declared `reports.Groups()` doc already filed p15.9 under `financial`, so no group-set change and the existing permission matrix picks up the auto-mounted route with zero new matrix code.
  - **NATIVE currency, per-currency rows (`Line | Currency | Without | With | Total`), NOT converted — a deliberate deviation from the p15.5 income statement's txn-date conversion, documented here.** The step permits native-or-converted "be consistent and document"; native is FORCED by the cross-report bridge: the DERIVED released line must equal **Σ p15.8 single-fund applied figures across the restricted funds by EXACT int64 equality** (`TestActivitiesReleasedMatchesFundStatements`), and p15.8 (`FundPeriodStatement`) is native. Converting would (a) break that exact equality and (b) need per-fund, per-MONTH activity the toolkit does not expose (`FundPeriodStatement` is whole-period native; `Activity` RateTxnDate is per-account, not per-fund). Multi-currency is shown one row per currency, exactly as the balance-sheet detail mode presents its by-restriction net-asset split.
  - **RESTRICTION-COLUMN classification is by the FUND a split lands in** (`Toolkit.restrictedFundIDs` = funds with `Restriction != ""`, the same rule as the balance sheet's `restrictedNetAssets`). **With-revenue** = Σ restricted funds' `Received` (from `FundPeriodStatement`, the −Σ revenue-splits positive display; a restricted liability draw would also count as restricted support, none in the fixture). **Without-revenue** = total revenue (`Activity` RateNone over revenue accounts, shown positive) − With-revenue, per currency — a whole-minus-restricted-part, so no separate NULL-fund query is needed. **Expenses** = all-fund `Activity` over expense accounts (positive net-debit), placed in Without only (functional expenses reduce unrestricted net assets AFTER the release).
  - **The "net assets released from restrictions" line is DERIVED (D20 — NO journaled transfer transactions exist)** = Σ restricted funds' APPLICATIONS in the period (`AppliedExpense + AppliedNonExpense` from `FundPeriodStatement`, so both an expense spend AND the Building purchase release restrictions). Presented **+released in Without, −released in With ⇒ the row NETS TO ZERO in Total** (it MOVES restricted resources to unrestricted as they are spent). **Change in net assets** per column = revenue ± released − expenses; **Without + With == Total by construction**, and **Total == revenue − expenses** (released nets out) — the per-currency analogue of "change == NetIncome" (`NetIncome` RateNone is single-currency-only, so the multi-currency fixture asserts per-currency instead; noted).
  - **HAND-VERIFIED numbers** (root scope, native, 2025-01-01..2026-06-30; golden `testdata/activities_by_restriction.{txt,csv}`). **USD:** revenue Without 6,950.00 (Contributions 2,750 + Program Fees 1,200 + Event 3,000) / With 52,000.00 (Building-Fund Contributions 50,000 + Beca GovGrants 2,000); **released 41,500.00** (Beca expense 1,500 + Building purchase 40,000), nets to zero; expenses 23,275.00; change Without 25,175.00 / With 10,500.00 / **Total 35,675.00 == 58,950 − 23,275** and == Without + With. **MXN:** revenue With 100,000.00 (Beca GovGrants), Without 0; **released 3,000.00** (Beca supplies), nets to zero; expenses 8,600.00; change Without −5,600.00 / With 97,000.00 / **Total 91,400.00**. `TestActivitiesReleasedMatchesFundStatements` asserts released == Σ p15.8 applications per currency (USD 4,150,000 / MXN 300,000, minor).
  - **DRILL wiring + a new `Drill.FundIDs` fund-SET (the one framework touch, p15.3d-adjacent, flagged as a deviation).** The released cell aggregates applications across EVERY restricted fund, so its USD figure spans TWO funds (Beca Agua 150,000 + Building Fund 4,000,000) — a single `*int64 FundID` cannot express it, and the store's `DrillFilter` has NO NULL-fund / fund-set predicate. Rather than change the SQL (scope creep on migrations/sqlc, p04.2-fragile), a `Drill.FundIDs []int64` was added (Encode/Decode round-trip tested) and the **web drill handler + the test helper loop `account SET × fund SET`, calling the EXISTING single-fund `DrillSplits` per pair** — pure Go composition, zero SQL change. The released drill targets **expense ∪ CAPITAL-asset accounts** (from `FundPeriodStatement.CapitalAccounts`, the Building), EXCLUDING cash/spendable assets — a cash debit on a grant receipt is not an application, so including cash would over-count by the fund's receipt/spend cash movements; non-restricted-fund splits on the same accounts (unrestricted expenses, the unrestricted Building opening) are filtered out by the fund set. `TestActivitiesReleasedDrillReconciles` reconciles USD 4,150,000 / MXN 300,000. The With-revenue cell drills the restricted funds' revenue splits (fund set); the Without-revenue cell is unrestricted (NULL fund) and left NON-drillable (the p15.8 fund-0 precedent); the expense cell drills the all-fund expense account set; Total cells (mixed roll-ups) and the structural-zero released Total are not drilled.
  - No new dependencies (stdlib `context`, `sort`), no new sqlc query (reuses `Activity`/`FundPeriodStatement`/`DrillSplits`/`ListFunds`/`Tree`); `go.mod`/`go.sum` unchanged. New i18n keys `reports.activities_by_restriction.{title,col.*,revenue,released,total_support,expenses,change}` in BOTH catalogs (all leaves, no dotted-key collision). `make lint test check` + `govulncheck ./...` exit 0 (the p06.1 informational `x/crypto/openpgp` finding persists); `make golden` no-diff. **e2e** `e2e/tests/reports.spec.js` (+1 test): seeds a restricted fund + a receipt into it + an unrestricted expense, opens the statement, sees the two restriction column headers + the revenue / released / expenses / change-in-net-assets rows + a grand-total row + a drill link, and fetches the CSV — STRICT CSP (no `page.waitForFunction`), MUTATES only unique-named rows (worker-db safe).

- **p15.10 (report: program statement — the decision-maker per-program view)** — Revenue/expense by natural account per PROGRAM (`internal/reports/program_statement.go`), the source p15.11 draws 990 Part III from, copying the p15.5 income-statement section/sign convention + the p15.3 golden + p15.3d drill patterns. Non-obvious calls:
  - **GROUP = `programs`** (the already-declared group `reports.Groups()` reserved for exactly this report). The route auto-mounts and the permission matrix picks it up with zero new matrix code.
  - **PER-ACCOUNT-PER-PROGRAM LAYOUT, per-currency rows: `Account | Currency | <program...>`.** Rows are natural leaf accounts grouped into a Revenue then an Expense section (pre-order within each), one row per (account, currency) present in any program column; a section-total row per currency; a **net-per-program line per currency** (revenue − expenses) at the foot. Revenue is displayed ×−1 (net-debit credit → positive inflow), expense ×+1 — the p15.5 income-statement convention exactly (`net = −(revNet + expNet)`).
  - **TREE ROLLUP: each program cell folds in its DESCENDANT programs (`Toolkit.ProgramActivity`, D24).** The seeded root "General" carries the whole org's program activity; e.g. General × Program Supplies USD 210,000 = 60,000 (General-direct) + 150,000 (Educación), Food Purchases MXN 360,000 = 210,000 + 150,000 (Food Pantry). Asserted against the RAW `f.Expected.Program` oracle (independent tally), not the report's own toolkit call.
  - **TWO PARAMETERIZATIONS via the new report-specific PROGRAM param (`Params.Program` / `ParamsSpec.Program`, mirroring Account/Fund; parsed+validated against `ProgramTree` in `web/reports.go`).** (1) **COMPARATIVE (default, no program):** one column per program in tree pre-order — General, Educación, Food Pantry — for side-by-side comparison. **The root (General) column IS the organization-wide total by construction (D24 single seeded root), so NO separate Total column is emitted** (it would duplicate the General column byte for byte). (2) **SINGLE SUBTREE (`?program=`):** that program (descendants rolled up) alone, `Account | Currency | <program name>` + net — the degenerate one-column case (the single money column's header is the chosen program's name, like every comparative column).
